**Strength of the Ram:** Your *Charge* damage increases by \+11 (3d6) kinetic damage, and the Dodge DC increases by 10\. Additionally, you gain another use of *Charge* per downtime.  
**Thundering Blow:** The force of your blow is now enough to knock your enemies off of their feet. If you make a successful melee attack, the target must make a DC 90 Fortitude interaction if they are a small creature, a DC 75 Fortitude interaction if they are a medium sized creature, and a DC 50 Fortitude interaction if they are a large creature. On a failure the target is pushed 10 feet away from you and exposed to the Fallen effect. Additionally, all of your melee attacks do an additional \+4d6 damage.  
**Last Stand**: When no other conscious allies are within 25 feet of you, you may make an additional weapon attack, and gain an additional Secondary and Tertiary Operation.

Field Marshal:  
**Hearty:** Add \+40 to base health.  
**Improved Shields:** Add \+24 to base shields.  
**Extended Grenade Belt:** Add \+2 grenade slots.  
**Extended Hip Holster:** Add \+2 gun slots.  
**Interaction Points:** You gain \+15 Interaction Points.

Lieutenant General:  
**Armor Lock:**  As a Primary Operation, you may enter into an armor lock where you stay for up to 2 turns or until you end it as a Secondary Operation. During this time you suffer a \-50 to all dodges and have your speed reduced to 0 feet, but you are immune to all damage and negative effects except that which the GM considers unreasonable (such as a nuclear explosion). When you exit armor lock any hostile creature within 5 feet of you must succeed on a Dodge DC 80 or take however much damage you took while armor locked as shock damage (Fortitude DC 60), taking half damage (rounded down) on a successful dodge. This can be done up to twice per downtime.  
**Wrist Rocket:** As a modification to your armor, you may add a small armament of miniature rockets into your wrist plating. The attachment is capable of holding up to 5 rockets at a time, regaining all rockets during downtime. As a Primary Operation, you can fire as many of these rockets at a target as you wish, with each rocket dealing 4d4 explosive damage with a Dodge DC 80\. This attack can be split between multiple targets. For example, if you fire 5 rockets, you can fire 2 at one enemy and 3 on another, or any other combination of your choice.  
**Repelling Pulse:** As a Secondary Operation you can activate a pulse from your armor for up to 3 turns, which can be ended at any point on your turn as no Operation. At the start of your turn any creatures within 20 feet of you must make a dodge or be pushed away. the Dodge DC of this attack and the amount they are pushed away depends on the creature’s size. Small creatures must make a Dodge DC 80 or be pushed 15 feet. Medium creatures must make a Dodge DC 65 or be pushed 10 feet. Large Creatures must make a Dodge DC 50 or be pushed 5 feet.                                                                                                                                        

General Major:  
**Juggernaut:** Your physical fortitude has allowed you to stretch the human body to its limit. Whenever you are knocked unconscious, you may instead choose to drop to 1 health instead. You may do this once per downtime for free, however for each time after, you must subtract \-5 from each of your rolls, and enemies get an additional \+5 to dodging your attacks. This penalty is cumulative, however if you reach a penalty of \-30, you are unable to regain consciousness via this ability again until the penalty is lessened or ends. After each downtime, you may take away up to 20 of this penalty.  
**Steel Will:** As a Secondary Operation you may forfeit your movement until the end of your next turn to take half damage (rounded down) from all attacks until the end of your next turn. This can be done 2 times per downtime.  
**Battering Ram:** Add an additional \+4d6 damage die to your *Charge* ability and gain 2 more uses of this ability per downtime. In addition, you have become an expert at dealing with multiple targets. You can now make your *Charge* attack against a second target within 5 feet of your initial target.

Commander:  
**Heart of a Lion:** Add \+60 to base health, and at the start of each of your turns you regain 5 health as long as you are conscious.  
**Shield of the People:** Add \+38 to your base shields, and once per downtime, you can bring yourself back to full shields as a Tertiary Operation.  
**Loose Cannon:** Add \+3 grenade slots, and the range of all grenades you throw is doubled.  
**Artillery Expert:** Add \+3 gun slots, and you may now take the Change Weapons Operation at will on your turn without having to spend a Tertiary Operation.  
**Interaction Points:** You gain \+25 Interaction Points.

Fleet Commander:  
**Jack of All Trades:** Select any two abilities of Commander rank or lower.  
**Diversified Tactics:** Select any ability from any class of Commander rank or lower, excluding Starting Abilities.  
**Berserker:** While below half of your maximum health, you take half damage (rounded down) from all attacks. Additionally, all melee attacks deal double damage while in this state.	

Hyper-Lethal Vector:  
**Seismic Charge:** Twice per downtime, as a Primary Operation, you can release a seismic charge originating from your character. You can force every hostile creature within 20 feet of you to make a DC 90 dodge or be exposed to the Fallen effect and take 8d10 kinetic damage, or half damage (rounded down) on a successful dodge.   
**Unwavering Defender:** Once per downtime, as a Secondary Operation, you can enter a state of heightened awareness that lasts for 5 minutes. During this time, you and all allies within 10 feet of you regain up to 5 health back at the start of each of their turns, and may increase the damage of all their weapon attacks by one die.

## Leader

As explosions sound in the distance, a Spartan rises from her trench and leads a charge into a Promethean base, a squad of marines behind her. She runs forward, firing her Battle Rifle with deadly precision, her spartans working in unison to overpower the enemy in moments. Receiving the next objective from her superior, she prepares to earn her squad to yet another victory. She is a leader, master tactician skilled in both offense and defense. Leaders are the driving force behind every fireteam. Other Spartans might have opinions on what to do, but the Leader calls the shots.

**Statistics:**   
Health: 35  
Shields: 50  
Health per rank up: 5 (1d8)  
Speed: 30 feet  
Size: Medium  
Recommended Starting Weaponry: Battle Rifle, Magnum Pistol  
Superiorities: Firepower, History  
Expertises: Tactics, Charisma  
Gun Carrying Capacity: You have 3 gun slots  
Grenade Capacity: You have 6 grenade slots

**Starting Ability:** *Command*. Twice per downtime, as a Secondary Operation, you may command an ally to take a Primary Operation at the same time that you take yours. 

2nd Lieutenant:  
**Hearty:** Add \+7 to your base health.  
**Improved Shields:** Add \+4 to your base shields.  
**Extended Grenade Belt**: Add \+1 grenade slot.  
**Extended Hip Holster:** Add \+1 gun slot.  
**Interaction Points:** You gain \+5 Interaction Points.

1st Lieutenant:  
**Well-Rounded:** You may add \+2 damage to all weapon attacks.  
**Fast:** Gain an extra \+5 feet of movement speed.  
**Medic:** During a downtime, you can create up to 3 medpacs.

Captain:  
**Assist:** When someone attacks a creature you damaged during your last turn, each of your allies attacks deals an additional \+3 damage, and the target’s dodge is decreased by \-5.  
**Versatile:** Add \+10 to 2 interactions of your choice.  
**Stalwart:** You have a \+20 to interactions and dodges made to avoid the Frightened and Surprised effects.

Major:  
**Hearty:** Add \+10 to your base health.  
**Improved Shields:** Add \+7 to your base shields.  
**Extended Grenade Belt:** Add \+1 grenade slot.  
**Extended Hip Holster:** Add \+1 gun slot.  
**Interaction Points:** You gain \+10 Interaction Points.

Lieutenant Colonel:   
**Flank:** When making an attack against an enemy that did not make an attack against you on their previous turn, they have a \-5 to dodges and you deal an additional 1d4 damage of that weapon’s damage type per attack.  
**Flash Mines:** You can deploy 3 small flash mines per downtime, and each can be placed as a Secondary Operation. They can be stuck onto surfaces, buried, or thrown up to 20 feet, and can be detonated as a Tertiary Operation. Any creature within 5 feet of the mine must succeed on a DC 50 dodge or be exposed to the Deafened and Blinded effects until the end of your next turn.  
**Pilot:** You become much more efficient at using vehicles. Therefore, when in the driver seat of a vehicle, moving the vehicle becomes no Operation, using the Ram ability becomes a Tertiary Operation, and using the vehicle’s weapons becomes a Secondary Operation.

Colonel Major:  
**Inspirational Command:** 4 times per downtime, as a Reactive Operation, you may utter a command to a friendly creature other than yourself that can understand you that just made any d100 roll. The creature may now add the result of a d20 roll to their d100 roll..  
**Regeneration Field:** Twice per downtime as a Primary Operation you can throw down a regeneration field with a 10 foot radius. Any creatures of your choice within the field regenerate up to 15 health per turn. This field lasts for up to five turns or until you deactivate it as a Secondary Operation.  
**Relentless Command:** You may use your *Command* ability 3 times per downtime.

Field Marshal:  
**Hearty:** Add \+18 to base health.  
**Improved Shields:** Add \+14 to base shields.  
**Extended Grenade Belt:** Add \+2 grenade slots.  
**Extended Hip Holster:** Add \+2 gun slots.  
**Interaction Points:** You gain \+15 Interaction Points.

Lieutenant General:

During this time you suffer a \-50 to all dodges and have your speed reduced to 0 feet, but you are immune to all damage and negative effects except that which the GM considers unreasonable (such as a nuclear explosion). When you exit armor lock any hostile creature within 5 feet of you must succeed on a Dodge DC 80 or take however much damage you took while armor locked as shock damage (Fortitude DC 60), taking half damage (rounded down) on a successful dodge. This can be done up to twice per downtime.  
**Wrist Rocket:** As a modification to your armor, you may add a small armament of miniature rockets into your wrist plating. The attachment is capable of holding up to 5 rockets at a time, regaining all rockets during downtime. As a Primary Operation, you can fire as many of these rockets at a target as you wish, with each rocket dealing 4d4 explosive damage with a Dodge DC 80\. This attack can be split between multiple targets. For example, if you fire 5 rockets, you can fire 2 at one enemy and 3 on another, or any other combination of your choice.  
**Ace:** Pick 2 interactions from which you already have expertise/superiority, you gain a \+25 to these interactions. 

General Major:  
**Improved Command:** When using your *Command* ability, you can now target up to 2 allies at a time. Additionally, chosen creatures regain \+20 health and gain an additional \+10 movement speed on their turn.  
**Rallying Cry:** Twice per downtime as Primary Operation you can yell a rallying cry. When used, you become immune to all damage for 1 round (within reason, which is to say the GM’s discretion), and up to 3 allies within 30 feet of you are exposed to the Indomitable effect until the end of their next turn.  
**Target:** As a Secondary Operation you may target one creature of your choice, and all attacks against that target do an additional 1d6 damage, and the Dodge DC of these attacks increases by \+5. You may switch which creature is being targeted as a Secondary Operation. 

Commander:  
**Heart of a Lion:** Add \+35 to base health, and at the start of each of your turns you regain 5 health as long as you are conscious.  
**Shield of the People:** Add \+25 to your base shields, and once per downtime, you can bring yourself back to full shields as a Tertiary Operation.  
**Loose Cannon:** Add \+3 grenade slots, and the range of all grenades you throw is doubled.  
**Artillery Expert:** Add \+3 gun slots, and you may now take the Change Weapons Operation at will on your turn without having to spend a Tertiary Operation.  
**Interaction Points:** You gain \+25 Interaction Points.

Fleet Commander:  
**Jack of All Trades:** Select any two abilities of Commander rank or lower.  
**Diversified Tactics:** Select any ability from any class of Commander rank or lower, excluding Starting Abilities.  
**Master of the Many:** You gain a \+15 to all ability checks you do not have superiority or expertise in.

Hyper-Lethal Vector:   
**I Like You Guys…:** Your confidence on the battlefield stirs the hearts of your companions. Any allies within 30 feet of you gain one of the following effects while in combat, chosen by you at the start of each of your turns:  
\-You regain \+10 health per turn  
\-You gain \+15 feet of movement speed  
\-You gain \+15 to all dodges  
\-You gain \+5 (1d8) to all weapon attacks  
**But I Don’t Like Them:** Conversely, your confidence on the battlefield strikes fear into the heart of your enemies. Any hostile creatures within 30 feet of you suffer from one of the following effects while in combat, chosen by you at the start of each of your turns:  
\-DC 25 dodge or be stunned  
\-Subtract 10 from their dodges  
\-Subtract 5 (1d8) from all weapon attacks  
\-Subtract 10 feet of movement speed

## 

##  Sniper

A lone man sits in a sniper perch, waiting for his quarry to come into his sights. Camouflaged against the backdrop of his surroundings, not a single soul can see him. As a Covenant Zealot enters his sniper’s scope, he aims and pulls the trigger. This is the sniper, a long-range warrior capable of dealing immense damage without having to get near the fight.

**Statistics:**  
Health: 15  
Shields: 25  
Health per rank up: 3 (1d4)  
Speed: 35 feet  
Size: Medium  
Recommended Starting Weaponry: Sniper Rifle, Magnum Pistol  
Superiorities: Agility, Tech  
Expertises: Detection, Stealth  
Gun Carrying Capacity: You have 3 gun slots  
Grenade Capacity: You have 5 grenade slots

**Starting Ability:** *Precision Aim.* 5 times per downtime, when you make a ranged weapon attack, you may choose to use this ability to instantly kill an enemy that has up to 75 total health & shields remaining if the attack hits them. You must choose to do so before you make the attack.

2nd Lieutenant:  
**Hearty:** Add \+3 to your base health.  
**Improved Shields:** Add \+2 to your base shields.  
**Extended Grenade Belt**: Add \+1 grenade slot.  
**Extended Hip Holster:** Add \+1 gun slot.  
**Interaction Points:** You gain \+5 Interaction Points.

1st Lieutenant:  
**Fast:** Gain an extra \+5 feet of movement speed.  
**Suppressor:** Ranged weapon attacks you make cannot be heard by creatures further than 10 feet away from you.  
**Agile:** Add \+5 to all dodges.

Captain:  
**Sniper Expert:** When using a weapon with a called shot bonus of \+15, add an additional \+2 damage die to the attack.  
**Hip Fire:** When within 10 feet of an enemy, the Dodge DC of your weapon attacks increases by \+10.  
**Take Aim**: You forfeit your entire turn to take extra time to line up an attack. When you make an attack on your next turn, the Dodge DC increases by 40 and deals an additional \+4 damage die.

Major:  
**Hearty:** Add \+5 to your base health.  
**Improved Shields:** Add \+4 to your base shields.  
**Extended Grenade Belt:** Add \+1 grenade slot.  
**Extended Hip Holster:** Add \+1 gun slot.  
**Interaction Points:** You gain \+10 Interaction Points.

Lieutenant Colonel:  
**Camouflage:** When making a Stealth interaction to hide, you may add an additional \+15 to the roll. Additionally, all creatures have a \-10 to Detection interactions while attempting to locate you.  
**Cloaking Devices:** 3 times per downtime, you can place a cloaking device on an object that could fit inside a 3 ft x 3 ft x 3 ft cube. The object will then be invisible to the naked eye, visible only with thermal imaging or similar technology. The object will remain invisible for up to one hour or until the cloaking devices are deactivated. It can be activated or deactivated remotely if you are within 2 miles of the object, however, the device must be attached manually.   
**Thermal Imaging Goggles:** Twice per downtime, for a minute each, you can activate thermal imaging goggles in your helmet that allow you to see and locate the thermal imaging of any creature within 60 feet, penetrating only through light underbrush and similar obstructions. These goggles allow you to ignore any penalties imposed by fighting in darkness. You can also read the current health and strength of the shields on up to 5 creatures.

Colonel Major:  
**Ambush:** If you make an attack against a creature that is exposed to the Surprised effect, you may treat the attack as a called shot of your choice if the creature fails the dodge by any amount. Additionally, any creature you attack in this manner has an additional \-15 penalty to their dodge.  
**Flawless Aim:** You can instantly kill an enemy with up to 150 total base health and shields remaining as part of your Precision Aim ability.  
**Shotcaller:** When making a called shot, your weapon’s called shot bonus increases by \+5, However the dodge penalty for the called shot cannot be reduced beyond \-0. In addition, your called shots become more effective in the following ways:  
Leg Shots: The target’s speed is now decreased by \-20 feet  
Arm Shots: The target will now drop anything in their hands on a roll of 1 or 2\.  
Headshots: Add an additional \+3 damage die.

Field Marshal:  
**Hearty:** Add \+11 to base health.  
**Improved Shields:** Add \+9 to base shields.  
**Extended Grenade Belt:** Add \+2 grenade slots.  
**Extended Hip Holster:** Add \+2 gun slots.  
**Interaction Points:** You gain \+15 Interaction Points.

Lieutenant General:  
**Tripwire:** You have a tripwire that you can place as a Primary Operation, creating a line up to 20 feet long that requires a DC 85 detection check for someone who isn’t aware of its presence to find. Anyone who walks through  it must make a DC 80 dodge or be exposed to the fallen effect.  
**False Identity:** You have become skilled at the art of imitating others’ appearances. You can use an hour of downtime to transform your appearance into that of another creature of the same size category as you. At a glance, your appearance is indiscernible from that of which you are imitating, however upon closer inspection, some faults can be detected. When your disguise is inspected closely, you must make a Charisma check against the inspecting creature’s Detection check. On a success, they fall for your disguise, however, on a fail, the inspecting creature can see through the disguise.  
**Strike From the Shadows:**  When attacking a creature exposed to the Surprised effect, your first attack grants an extra amount of damage die equal to the base amount of weapon damage die.

General Major:  
**Armor Piercing Rounds:** 8 times per downtime, you may choose to use specialized armor piercing rounds. You must specify that you are using one of these rounds before you make your attack. When you choose to use these rounds, half of the damage dealt is dealt to the shields of a creature, while the other half is dealt to the base health. If this damage breaks the creatures’ shields, any extra is applied to the base health. If the creature has no shields, then it deals an extra 3 damage die to the specified target.  
**Penetrating Shot:** When attacking a creature, if the damage of your attack exceeds the health of that creature, the remaining damage can be transferred to another creature within a 15 foot line behind the defeated creature. The second creature must then make a dodge with 15 subtracted from the weapons Dodge DC. If the creature fails, then they take half of the remaining damage. It is possible for this damage to pierce through multiple enemies.  
**Small Weapons Expert:** After using your Primary Operation, you can switch to a single small weapon expending a Secondary and Tertiary Operation. You may then make up to 3 attacks with that weapon, however it cannot exceed the maximum number of times that weapon can be fired in a turn as described in its statistics. You then have the option to swap your weapon again using no Operation.

Commander:  
**Heart of a Lion:** Add \+18 to base health, and at the start of each of your turns you regain 5 health as long as you are conscious.  
**Shield of the People:** Add \+15 to your base shields, and once per downtime, you can bring yourself back to full shields as no Operation.  
**Loose Cannon:** Add \+3 grenade slots, and the range of all grenades you throw is doubled.  
**Artillery Expert:** Add \+3 gun slots, and you may now take the Change Weapons Operation at will on your turn without having to spend a Tertiary Operation.  
**Interaction Points:** You gain \+25 Interaction Points.

Fleet Commander:  
**Jack of All Trades:** Select any two abilities of Commander rank or lower.  
**Diversified Tactics:** Select any ability from any class of Commander rank or lower, excluding Starting Abilities.  
**Off the Grid:** You cannot be detected by any technology that reveals your location (radar, thermal imaging goggles, etc).

Hyper-Lethal Vector:  
**Sonar:** The built-in sonar module in your helmet makes you aware of the location of all creatures without an active camo module within 30 feet of you. When attempting to shoot through a barrier targeting creature that you can locate with your sonar, you may treat that barrier as 3 levels lower than its stated level.   
**Ricochet:** You have gained the ability to ricochet your shots off of applicable surfaces. After each ricochet, roll a d100. If you get below the number specified in the table below, the shot cannot ricochet off of any more surfaces. The range of the weapon is unaffected by the number of times the bullet ricochets on an object. The different surfaces that the shot can be ricocheted off of and their penalties are as follows:

Flimsy: cannot ricochet  
Weak: \-25 to weapon’s dodge, 60 or above to continue ricochet  
Average: \-20 to weapon’s dodge, 50 or above to continue ricochet  
Sturdy: \-15 to weapon’s dodge, 40 or above to continue ricochet  
Solid: \-10 to weapon’s dodge, 30 or above to continue ricochet  
Strong: \-5 to weapon’s dodge, 20 or above to continue ricochet  
Unassailable: weapon’s dodge unaffected, 10 or above to continue ricochet

## Tech

A hacker sits at her computer attempting to upload a virus into the enemies’ security system. Her fingers are flying as everything from cameras to turrets start to come offline. She shuts off her computer as the entire security system comes crashing down around her. This is the Tech, a technologically savvy supporter who has the ability to hack both her allies’, or her enemies’ shields.

**Statistics:**  
Health: 35  
Shields: 40  
Health per rank up: 5 (1d8)  
Speed: 35 feet  
Size: Medium  
Recommended Starting Weaponry: 2 Magnum Pistols  
Superiorities: History, Medicinal  
Expertises: Handling, Tech  
Gun Carrying Capacity: You have 2 gun slots  
Grenade Capacity: You have 4 grenade slots

**Starting Ability:** *Shield Recharge.* 5 times per downtime, you can use your Secondary Operation to recharge the shields of an ally within 30 ft of you and restore their shields by half (rounded down). You can restore your own shields in this way too.

2nd Lieutenant:  
**Hearty:** Add \+7 to your base health.  
**Improved Shields:** Add \+5 to your base shields.  
**Extended Grenade Belt**: Add \+1 grenade slot.  
**Extended Hip Holster:** Add \+1 gun slot.  
**Interaction Points:** You gain \+5 Interaction Points.

1st Lieutenant:  
**Agile:** Add \+5 to all dodges.  
**Medic:** During a downtime, you can create up to 3 medpacs.  
**Disable:** As a Secondary Operation you can disable any simple electronic device that you could normally influence with the Tech interaction within 20 feet of you for up to 1 minute. 

Captain:  
**Tech Expert:** Add an additional \+15 to all Tech and Handling interactions.  
**Listening Device:** You are given a total of 5 listening devices, capable of picking up sound audibly in a 30 foot radius. They are small, only a few inches across and long, and can be attached to any solid surface. While within one mile of a listening device, you are aware of all sounds made in the 30 foot radius.  If one is lost or destroyed, you may spend the next downtime creating up to 5 new listening devices, with a maximum of 5 listening devices carried  
**Medical Foam:** As a Secondary Operation, you may target one dying creature within 5 feet. Any creature you target in this way is stabilized and no longer suffers repeat damage from the attack that downed them. This effect lasts for up to an hour, or until damage equal to half (rounded down) of that creature’s base health is dealt to them.

Major:  
**Hearty:** Add \+11 to your base health.  
**Improved Shields:** Add \+8 to your base shields.  
**Extended Grenade Belt:** Add \+1 grenade slot.  
**Extended Hip Holster:** Add \+1 gun slot.  
**Interaction Points:** You gain \+10 Interaction Points.

Lieutenant Colonel:  
**Anti-Gravity Armor:** Once per day you can activate a series of anti-gravity thrusters for up to ten minutes. These thrusters limit your speed to your base speed minus 5, however you can now walk on any surface, such as walls and ceilings. Additionally, difficult terrain does not limit your movement speed and you cannot take fall damage while this is active.  
**Thermal Imaging Goggles:** Twice per downtime, for a minute each, you can activate thermal imaging goggles in your helmet that allow you to see and locate the thermal imaging of any creature within 60 feet, penetrating only through light underbrush and similar obstructions. These goggles allow you to ignore any penalties imposed by fighting in darkness. You can also read the current health and strength of the shields on up to 5 creatures.  
**Doctor:** When using a medpac, the health regained is now equal to the amount rolled on a medicinal check, adding all bonuses.

Colonel Major:  
**EMP:** 3 times per downtime, as Primary Operation, you may use an EMP grenade. The grenade can be thrown up to 30 feet, and has a radius of 10 feet. Any creatures or vehicles within that range must make a DC 85 dodge or be exposed to the Stunned effect. Any vehicle caught in the radius must complete a DC 60 dodge or be rendered immobile and unable to fire any weapons other than turrets. The stunned effect lasts for 3 rounds, or until the creature completes the dodge, which they may remake as a Primary Operation at the end of each of their turns, with the Dodge DC decreasing by ten each turn it is active. Additionally, at the end of each of the creature’s turns that it spends in the radius, regardless of whether it made the dodge or not, they take an additional 9 (2d8) shock damage but do not have to make a Fortitude interaction against the Stunned effect.  
**Restoration:** When using your *Shield Recharge*, you can remove up to two effects from the target creature, other than the wounded and unconscious effects. When you choose this ability, you gain an additional use of *Shield Recharge* per downtime.  
**Swift Action:** Twice per downtime, as a Secondary Operation, you can hack into the armor of an ally within 20 feet and grant them greater freedom of movement. The chosen ally gains an additional \+10 movement speed and an additional \+15 to all dodges for up to one minute.

Field Marshal:  
**Hearty:** Add \+20 to base health.  
**Improved Shields:** Add \+15 to base shields.  
**Extended Grenade Belt:** Add \+2 grenade slots.  
**Extended Hip Holster:** Add \+2 gun slots.  
**Interaction Points:** You gain \+15 Interaction Points.

Lieutenant General:  
**Tripwire:** You have a tripwire that you can place as a Primary Operation, creating a line up to 20 feet long that requires a DC 85 detection check for someone who isn’t aware of its presence to find. Anyone who walks through  it must make a DC 80 dodge or be exposed to the fallen effect.  
**Immunity to Effects:** As a Tertiary Operation you may cleanse an ally from 1 effect other than wounded.  
**Tactical Advantage:** As a Reactive Operation, when an ally within 30 feet of you makes a dodge you may add a \+20 to the dodge. You must choose to do this before the dodge roll is made.   
    
General Major:  
**Weapon Upgrade:** Once per downtime, you may select one weapon of your choice to upgrade. You may choose three of the following benefits for the upgraded weapon:  
\-Add an additional \+1 damage die.  
\-Increase the range of the weapon by half (rounded down).  
\-Add an additional \+2 Ammo Die.  
\-Increase the Dodge DC of the weapon by 10\.  
\-Make an additional attack provided that the weapon has more than one attack.  
**Vehicle Rewire:** Twice per downtime, you can use a Primary Operation to rewire a vehicle's hardware to rig it to explode at a time of your choosing. After rewiring the vehicle, you may choose to detonate the bomb anywhere between 1-5 rounds after the Operation. Until the designated time of explosion, the vehicle operates as normal.  
**The Tech Giveth and the Tech Taketh:** Your Shield Recharge ability now fully restores the shields of the ally it targets, and in addition, when you use this ability, you may choose one enemy within 30 feet of you and reduce their current shields by \-3d10.

Commander:  
**Heart of a Lion:** Add \+30 to base health, and at the start of each of your turns you regain 5 health as long as you are conscious.  
**Shield of the People:** Add \+25 to your base shields, and once per downtime, you can bring yourself back to full shields as no Operation.  
**Loose Cannon:** Add \+3 grenade slots, and the range of all grenades you throw is doubled.  
**Artillery Expert:** Add \+3 gun slots, and you may now take the Change Weapons Operation at will on your turn without having to spend a Tertiary Operation.  
**Interaction Points:** You gain \+25 Interaction Points.

Fleet Commander:  
**Jack of All Trades:** Select any two abilities of Fleet Commander rank or lower.  
**Diversified Tactics:** Select any ability from any class of Commander rank or lower, excluding Starting Abilities.  
**Retaliatory Surge:** As a Reactive Operation, after all of your shield health has been depleted, you release a surge of energy centered around yourself. Any target of your choice within 20 feet must succeed on a DC 85 dodge or take 28 (5d10) shock damage with a DC 65 Fortitude interaction.

Hyper-Lethal Vector:  
**Overclock**: Once per downtime, you can boost the combat abilities of an ally who is within 50 feet of you beyond their normal limits for up to one minute. The effects of this boost are as follows:  
\-Double their shield health.  
\-They gain an additional Primary Operation on each of their turns.  
\-Add an additional \+2 damage die to all attacks.  
**Disarming Frequency:** 3 times per downtime, you can use a Secondary Operation to disable one creature’s weapon or vehicle up to 60 ft away for 1d4 turns by emitting a frequency from your helmet’s comlink that renders the weapon useless. While the weapon is disabled, it cannot be fired normally or be used in any way except for those that a hunk of metal could be used for. While a vehicle is disabled, the pilot of the vehicle cannot take any Operations with the vehicle and the vehicle’s speed is reduced to 0\. Flying vehicles will plummet as a result, as long as there is a source of gravity.

## Tracker

Scouting ahead of the rest of the fireteam, the Tracker aims to gather valuable information as to their enemies’ position. Able to sniff out anything without making a sound, she sees through the Covenant raiding party’s camouflage. Quietly coming from behind with a silenced DMR, she takes out the sentries as she aims her final shot into the head of their leader.

**Statistics:**  
Health: 30  
Shields: 40  
Health per rank up: 4 (1d6)  
Speed: 40 feet  
Size: Medium  
Recommended Starting Weaponry: DMR, Magnum Pistol  
Superiorities: Medicinal, Detection  
Expertises: Tracking, Stealth  
Gun Carrying Capacity: You have 2 gun slots  
Grenade Capacity: You have 5 grenade slots

**Starting Ability:** *Scout.* Your armor is infused with a small active camo module. Once per downtime, as a Primary Operation, you can become exposed to the Invisible effect, which lasts for up to 10 minutes, or until you deactivate it as a Secondary Operation, make a weapon attack or make a combat maneuver.

2nd Lieutenant:  
**Hearty:** Add \+5 to your base health.  
**Improved Shields:** Add \+3 to your base shields.  
**Extended Grenade Belt**: Add \+1 grenade slot.  
**Extended Hip Holster:** Add \+1 gun slot.  
**Interaction Points:** You gain \+5 Interaction Points.

1st Lieutenant:  
**Fast:** Gain an extra \+5 movement speed.  
**Suppressor:** Ranged weapon attacks you make cannot be heard by creatures further than 10 feet away from you.   
**Agile:** Add \+5 to all dodges.

Captain:  
**Covert Adept:** You can use your *Scout* ability twice per downtime instead of once.  
**Climbing Spikes:** You may climb up vertical surfaces with no penalty to movement.  
**Expert Survivalist:** Add an additional \+15 to all Tracking and Detection interactions. 

Major:   
**Hearty:** Add \+9 to your base health.  
**Improved Shields:** Add \+7 to your base shields.  
**Extended Grenade Belt:** Add \+1 grenade slot.  
**Extended Hip Holster:** Add \+1 gun slot.  
**Interaction Points:** You gain \+10 Interaction Points.

Lieutenant Colonel:  
**Camouflage:** When making a Stealth interaction to hide, you may add an additional \+15 to the roll. Additionally, all creatures have a \-10 to Detection interactions while attempting to locate you.  
**Cloaking Devices:** 3 times per downtime, you can place a cloaking device on an object that could fit inside a 3 ft x 3 ft x 3 ft cube. The object will then be invisible to the naked eye, visible only with thermal imaging or similar technology. The object will remain invisible for up to one hour or until the cloaking devices are deactivated. It can be activated or deactivated remotely if you are within 2 miles of the object, however, the device must be attached manually.   
**Thermal Imaging Goggles:** Twice per downtime, for a minute each, you can activate thermal imaging goggles in your helmet that allow you to see and locate the thermal imaging of any creature within 60 feet, penetrating only through light underbrush and similar obstructions. These goggles allow you to ignore any penalties imposed by fighting in darkness. You can also read the current health and strength of the shields on up to 5 creatures.

Colonel Major:  
**Tracer Rounds:** Each turn you may designate a single attack with a weapon that deals kinetic, plasma, or hardlight damage as being a tracer round. If this attack hits the target, then the outline of the target can be seen through walls and other objects from up to 80 feet away for the next hour.   
**Even the Odds:** If you make a weapon attack while exposed to the Invisible effect, the attack automatically deals an additional \+4 damage die. Additionally, if using a precision weapon, Add \+10 to the weapon’s Dodge DC when calling a shot. The attack still ends the Invisible effect as normal.  
**Improved Invisibility:** When using *Scout*, the Invisible effect now lasts for up to an hour, you gain \+10 to Stealth interactions while exposed to the Invisible effect, and you may use the Disarm, Switch and Grapple maneuvers without ending the Invisible effect. 

Field Marshal:  
**Hearty:** Add \+13 to base health.  
**Improved Shields:** Add \+11 to base shields.  
**Extended Grenade Belt:** Add \+2 grenade slots.  
**Extended Hip Holster:** Add \+2 gun slots.  
**Interaction Points:** You gain \+15 Interaction Points.

Lieutenant General:  
**Tripwire:** You have a tripwire that you can place as a Primary Operation, creating a line up to 20 feet long that requires a DC 85 detection check for someone who isn’t aware of its presence to find. Anyone who walks through  it must make a DC 80 dodge or be exposed to the fallen effect.  
**False Identity:** You have become skilled at the art of imitating others’ appearances. You can use an hour of downtime to transform your appearance into that of another creature of the same size category as you. At a glance, your appearance is indiscernible from that of which you are imitating, however upon closer inspection, some faults can be detected. When your disguise is inspected closely, you must make a Charisma check against the inspecting creature’s Detection check. On a success, they fall for your disguise, however, on a failure, the inspecting creature can see through the disguise.  
**Strike From the Shadows:** When attacking a creature exposed to the Surprised effect, your first attack grants an extra amount of damage die equal to the base weapon damage.

General Major:  
**Hand to Hand Combatant:** While exposed to the Invisible effect, you may make an additional melee attack as part of your Primary Operation.  
**Ghillie Suit:** You can spend an hour constructing a ghillie suit according to an environment of your choice. When in the environment that it is designed for, you gain an additional \+20 to Stealth interactions and dodges. It takes a Primary Operation to put on or take off the suit. You may have no more than 1 ghillie suit in your possession at a time.  
**Bear Trap:** You have 2 bear traps that can be planted or buried anywhere you wish. Any creature of size large or smaller that steps on the trap, provided that there is no more than a foot of any material covering it, must succeed on a Dodge DC 95 or take 5d8 kinetic damage and be exposed to the Incapacitated effect. To end this effect, the creature must use a Primary Operation to attempt a DC 55 Lifting interaction to disarm the trap, or deal 20 damage to it.

Commander:  
**Heart of a Lion:** Add \+23 to base health, and at the start of each of your turns you regain 5 health as long as you are conscious.  
**Shield of the People:** Add \+19 to your base shields, and once per downtime, you can bring yourself back to full shields as no Operation.  
**Loose Cannon:** Add \+3 grenade slots, and the range of all grenades you throw is doubled.  
**Artillery Expert:** Add \+3 gun slots, and you may now take the Change Weapons Operation at will on your turn without having to spend a Tertiary Operation.  
**Interaction Points:** You gain \+25 Interaction Points.

Fleet Commander:  
**Jack of All Trades:** Select any two abilities of Commander rank or lower.  
**Diversified Tactics:** Select any ability from any class of Commander rank or lower, excluding Starting Abilities.  
**Off the Grid:** You cannot be detected by any technology that reveals your location (radar, thermal imaging goggles, etc).

Hyper-Lethal Vector  
**Expert Tracker:** You have honed your abilities to the maximum allowed by the human species. You gain the following benefits permanently:  
\-You gain \+15 to all dodges.  
\-You gain \+15 to movement speed.  
\-You gain \+10 to all Tracking interactions.  
\-While invisible, you can take up to 40 damage before the effect ends.  
\-Add \+5 to all Dodge DCs for called shots.  
**Lone Wolf:** When attacking an enemy in direct line of sight, with no creatures within 15 feet of either you or your target, you gain the following benefits against only that creature. These do not apply when attacking or being attacked by another creature.  
\-You may make an additional attack with any weapon of large size or smaller  
\-Add \+10 to all Dodge DCs for called shots   
\-All attacks deal an extra \+6 (1d10) damage  
\-You gain a \+20 to all dodges

# 

# Homeworlds & Backgrounds

Spartans hail from all across Earth’s colonies. Each Spartan is shaped by their experiences on their Homeworld. These Spartans come from unique backgrounds that can influence the way they see and interact with their environment. As part of Character Creation, you will select a Homeworld and a Background to represent your Character’s life before they were inducted into the Spartan program. 

**Urban** \- An Urban Homeworld consists of a dense population in a metropolitan community. You are accustomed to skyscrapers, alleyways, streets, and the finest architectural achievements humanity has to offer.   
**Agrarian** \- An Agrarian Homeworld consists of rural farmlands. You are accustomed to farm life, living away from civilization, and living off the land.    
**Forested** \- A Forested Homeworld is composed of undeveloped woodlands, jungles, or rainforests. You are accustomed to hunting, survivalism, a low level of technology, and wild, unspoiled wilderness.  
**Oceanic** \- An Oceanic Homeworld is in part or completely covered by deep water. You are accustomed to marine life, sailing, stormy weather, and the unpredictable temperament of the sea.   
**Cosmic** \- A Cosmic Homeworld is a Homeworld that is exposed to the vacuum of space, such as a Space Station or Asteroid Colony. You are accustomed to confined spaces, advanced technology, space travel, and the constant looming threat of death.  
**Arid** \- An Arid Homeworld has little rainfall, such as a tundra or desert. You are accustomed to extreme climates, dry and barren landscapes, limited resources, and living within inhospitable ecosystems. 

Each Homeworld comes with its own unique benefits, as well as a choice of backgrounds that all represent upbringings unique to these planets. 

**Urban**  
When Piloting a vehicle in an urban environment, you have a \+5 bonus to Dodge Rolls and a \+10 bonus to the vehicle’s movement speed. In addition, entering and exiting a vehicle for you is a Secondary Operation in Urban environments. 

*Architect* \- Add \+10 to Crafting interactions and when shooting through cover, you may treat the cover as being one level lower.

*Criminal* \- Add \+10 to Stealth interactions and when dual-wielding weapons you may make one extra attack with your second weapon.

*Socialite* \- Add \+10 to Charisma interactions and when making a roll to interact with a friendly creature that can understand you, you may roll 2d100 and use the higher roll. 

**Agrarian**  
When in an agrarian environment, any cover you are behind counts as 1 level higher.

*Farmer \-* Add \+10 to Fortitude interactions and you may take the Grapple maneuver without spending a Primary Operation. 

*Pioneer \-* Add \+10 to Detection interactions and a \+5 Dodge Bonus when more than 30 feet away from any allies.

*Laborer \-* Add \+25 to Lifting interactions.

**Forested**   
When in a forested environment, you gain \+10 movement speed. 

*Hunter:* Add \+10 to Tracking interactions and you deal an additional \+1 damage die against any creature you succeed on a Tracking interaction against while following. 

*Naturalist*: Add \+10 to Medicinal interactions and when making Medicinal interactions to use medpacks you may roll 2d100 and use the higher roll. 

*Explorer:* Add \+10 to Agility interactions and ignore difficult terrain caused by natural effects. 

**Oceanic**  
When in an oceanic environment, when in water at least waist-deep, you can ignore penalties imposed by difficult terrain and treat the water as average cover. 

*Sailor* \- Add \+10 to Tactics interactions and allies within 10 feet of you with a Dodge Bonus lower than yours may use your Dodge Bonus when making Dodge Rolls. 

*Diver* \- Add \+10 to Agility Interactions and ignore movement and dodge penalties when submerged in water.

*Salvager* \- Add \+10 to Crafting Interactions and you may spend an hour crafting up to 3 ammo die for a small weapon, 2 ammo die for a medium weapon, or 1 ammo die for a large weapon.

**Cosmic**  
When in a cosmic environment, you can ignore the movement penalties associated with combat in space. 

*Technician* \- You can spend 2 hours making a machine that will help with one interaction of your choice. The machine will add a \+10 to the roll. You can have up to 2 machines active at a time.

*Astronaut* \- Add \+10 to all Handling interactions and can spend 10 minutes to repair a vehicle for up to 20 health. 

*Soldier* \- Add \+10 to Firepower interactions and as a Secondary Operation, you can make a DC 90 Tactics interaction to see if you can correctly predict where a certain enemy will move next. On a successful interaction, your weapon’s Dodge DC increases by \+10 against that creature until the end of your turn

**Arid**  
When in an arid environment, you can ignore the penalties of the first two levels of exhaustion.  However, when you reach the third level of exhaustion, the penalties of the first two are cumulative. 

*Athlete \-* Add \+10 to Agility interactions and \+10 to movement speed.

*Nomad \-* Add \+10 to Detection interactions and the Scramble maneuver does not cost your Secondary Operation.

*Exile:* Add \+10 to Fortitude interactions and \+10 to Demolition interactions and you cannot be killed by exhaustion. 

# Weapons and Vehicles

**![][image3]**

## WEAPON STATISTICS

**Damage**: The amount of damage each weapon deals.  
**Dodge:** The Dodge DC of attacks made with the weapon.  
**Size:** The size of the weapon.  
**Type:** The damage type of a weapon.  
**Ammo Die:** The amount and type of ammo die the weapon uses.  
**Attacks:** The number of attacks the weapon may make each turn.  
**Dual-Wield:** This indicates whether the weapon can be dual wielded or not.  
**Precision Weapon:** This indicates whether the weapon is a precision weapon or not.  
**Called Shot Bonus:** The weapon’s bonus to called shots.  
**Cover Negation:** The level of cover the weapon can negate. This applies only to the damage die penalties and not the dodge bonuses granted to creatures behind cover. The damage die penalty increases by 1 for every level of cover beyond the level of cover the weapon can negate.  
**Range:** The range of the weapon.  
**Special Ability:** Any abilities the weapon has that aren’t universal among all weapons.

Ammo Die  
Each weapon has a certain amount of ammo die. Anytime a creature makes an attack with a weapon they roll one of the weapon’s ammo die. When a 1 is rolled, the weapon loses that ammo die and the creature must use a Secondary Operation to reload that weapon on their next turn. When a weapon loses all of its ammo die, it can no longer be used until more ammo for the weapon is found. Usually the GM does not roll ammo dice.

Attacking Beyond Range  
When making an attack beyond the range of a weapon, the Dodge DC decreases by 15 for every 5 feet beyond the weapon’s range. For precision weapons, the Dodge DC only decreases by 10 for every 5 feet beyond the weapon’s range. When the Dodge DC of the weapon reaches 0, the attack automatically misses.

### 

### UNSC WEAPONRY

Grappling Hook  
Damage: N/A  
Dodge: DC 60  
Size: Small  
Type: N/A  
Ammo Die: N/A  
Attacks: 1  
Dual-Wield: N/A  
Precision Weapon: No  
Called Shot Bonus: N/A  
Cover Negation: Flimsy  
Range: 40 feet

**Special Abilities:**  
*Attach:* You can use your Primary Operation to attach your Grappling Hook to a point or object within range. If you attempt to attach to a creature instead, the creature must make a Dodge against the Dodge DC of the grappling hook. Until you use a Tertiary Operation to release the Grappling Hook neither you nor the target can be more than 40 feet apart. If the target is an object of less than 30 pounds or a creature of your size or smaller that fails a Lifting interaction against your own Lifting interaction, it will follow you at a speed equal to yours to remain within 40 feet of you.   
*Approach:* As a Secondary Operation, you can instantly move up to 40 feet closer (or, if the target is an object of 30 pounds or less or a creature of your size or smaller that fails a Lifting interaction against you, move the object up to 40 feet closer to you) to a target you have already attached to. If traveling towards a targeted creature or object in this way brings you into melee range, you may make a single melee Punch attack against the target as a Tertiary Operation. If you travel within 5 feet of a vehicle in this way, you may make the necessary Agility or Handling interaction necessary for hijacking expending no Operations provided that there is no cockpit or that it has been sufficiently damaged.  
*Built-in:* The Grappling Hook does not use a Tertiary Operation to switch to.

Magnum Pistol  
Damage: 11 (3d6)  
Dodge: DC 65  
Size: Small  
Type: Kinetic  
Ammo Die: 6d4  
Attacks: 2  
Dual-Wield: Yes  
Precision Weapon: Yes  
Called Shot Bonus: \+5  
Cover Negation: Weak  
Range: 50 feet

Attacks: 1  
Dual Wield: No  
Precision Weapon: No  
Called Shot Bonus: N/A  
Cover Negation: Flimsy  
Range: 15 feet

**Special Abilities:**   
*Sticky*: The projectiles of this weapon attach themselves to objects or creatures that they hit, requiring a DC 65 Lifting check to remove if they do not explode outright. If the attack misses the target creature, the projectile becomes attached to an unoccupied space up to 10 feet behind them.   
*Charge Up:* If you hit a creature or object with this weapon, you can use Primary Operation to charge it up, doing more damage. For each Operation you charge it up, it will deal an additional \+11 (2d10) explosive damage to a maximum of \+50 (9d10) additional Explosive damage. Once it reaches this point, it explodes immediately. Additionally, you can use a Secondary Operation to detonate it anytime beforehand on your turn.   
*Detonation:* Any creature within 5 feet of the detonation must make a dodge or take half damage (rounded down), taking no damage on a success.

## TURRET STATISTICS

Turrets are similar to guns, and can save a desperate fireteam when in need. Turrets are larger projectile weapons that are mounted on a fixed base, but can be detached by a suitably strong combatant, such as a Spartan. They follow the same rules as other weapons, with a few unique traits listed below. 

**Damage**: The amount of damage each turret deals.  
**Dodge:** The Dodge DC of attacks made with the turret.  
**Size:** The size of the turret.  
**Type:** The damage type of a turret.  
**Ammo Die:** The amount and type of ammo die the turret uses while not mounted.  
**Attacks:** The number of attacks a turret may make each turn.  
**Dual-Wield:** This indicates whether a gun can be dual wielded or not.  
**Precision Weapon:** This indicates whether a turret is a precision weapon or not.  
**Called Shot Bonus:** The turret’s bonus to called shots.  
**Cover Negation:** The level of cover the turret can negate. This applies only to the damage die penalties and not the dodge bonuses granted to creatures behind cover. The damage die penalty increases by 1 for every level of cover beyond the level of cover the turret can negate.  
**Range:** The range of the turret.  
**Special Ability:** Any abilities the turret has that aren’t universal among all turrets.

Mounted and Detached Turrets  
Turrets have two modes; mounted and detached. A mounted turret refers to one that is stationary, while a detached turret refers to one that is actively being carried around by someone. As a Tertiary Operation you may start or stop using a turret that is mounted. While a turret is mounted, it does not consume ammo, and you may make an additional attack, but lose the ability to move and make combat maneuvers while operating the turret. Despite not being able to move a mounted turret, it can still fire in all directions. As a Secondary Operation, you may detach the turret, provided that you have the necessary gun slots. When a turret is detached it becomes portable, however the user loses 10 feet of movement speed and the ability to make the Dash, Evasion, and Scramble maneuvers.

*Detonation: T*he target creature must make a dodge or take full damage, taking half damage (rounded down) on a success. Any creature within 5 feet of the detonation must make a dodge or take half damage (rounded down), taking no damage on a success.

## GRENADE STATISTICS

As a Primary Operation, you may arm and throw a grenade. Many of the grenades have different uses and can be applied to a variety of different scenarios and situations. The statistics of grenades are as follows:

Statistics  
**Damage:** The amount of damage each grenade deals.  
**Dodge:** The Dodge DC of the grenade.  
**Type:** The damage type of the grenade.  
**Radius:** The size of the grenade’s radius.  
**Range:** How far the grenade can be thrown without penalty.  
**Special Abilities:** Any abilities the grenade has that aren’t universal among all grenades.

Radius  
The size of the radius determines how many creatures or objects can be hit by a grenade. When you use a grenade, you may select one creature as the target. On a failed dodge, that target takes the full damage of the grenade, taking only half damage (rounded down) on a success. Any other creatures within the grenade’s radius must also make the dodge, taking half damage (rounded down) on a failed dodge and no damage on a success. 

Throwing Beyond Range  
When attempting to throw a grenade beyond its range, the Dodge DC of the grenade decreases by 5 for every 5 feet beyond the grenade’s range that it is being thrown.

In-Hand Detonation  
If you choose to detonate a grenade while you are within 5 feet of the target, the Dodge DC of the grenade increases by 35, but you are exposed to the grenade’s blast as well, taking half damage (rounded down) on a failed dodge and no damage on a success.

## GRENADES

Fragmentation Grenade  
Damage: 28 (5d10)  
Dodge: DC 55  
Type: Explosive  
Radius: 5 feet  
Range: 20 feet

**Special Abilities:**   
N/A

Plasma Grenade  
Damage: 10d4   
Dodge: DC 50  
Type: Explosive  
Radius: 5 feet  
Range: 25 feet

**Special Abilities:**   
*Adhesive:* When throwing a Plasma Grenade you can attempt to stick it to the target. If you do so, the Dodge DC is reduced by \-10, but if the target (and other targets within the radius) fail their save, they take an additional \+5d4 damage. 

Pulse Grenade  
Damage: 13 (2d12)  
Dodge: DC 35  
Type: Hardlight  
Radius: 5 feet  
Range: 25 feet

**Special Abilities:**   
For the next 2 rounds, the Pulse Grenade creates a 5 ft by 5 ft space centered on the target. When a creature enters or starts its turn in this space, it takes 13 (2d12) damage. 

Stun Grenade  
Damage: 7 (2d6)  
Dodge: DC 50  
Type: Shock (Fortitude DC 50\)  
Radius: 10 feet  
Range: 20 feet

**Special Abilities:**   
*Immobilize:* Any vehicles that fail the dodge lose all movement speed and pilot Operations, however any turrets and passenger functions remain unaffected. This lasts until the end of the user’s next turn.

Incendiary Grenade  
Damage: 11 (2d10)  
Dodge: 35  
Type: Thermal  
Radius 10 feet  
Range: 25 feet

**Special Abilities:**  
*Ignite:* Any flammable objects within the radius catch fire and deal an additional \+3 (1d4) thermal damage when touched or interacted with.

Smoke Grenade  
Damage: N/A  
Dodge: N/A  
Type: N/A  
Radius 5 feet  
Range: 35 feet

**Special Abilities:**  
*Obscure:* The smoke grenade obscures everything in its radius; creatures cannot see into or past the radius of the smoke grenade. All creatures within radius of the grenade gain an additional \+10 dodge bonus as they are engulfed in smoke, however suffer \-10 Dodge DC to any attacks they make while in the smoke. Creatures with Thermal Imaging Goggles and similar technology may make attacks as normal. This smoke lasts for a minute.

## VEHICLE STATISTICS

Vehicles are larger than people, and will have a harder time avoiding bullet fire. The severity of this penalty is directly proportional to the size of the vehicle. The table below lists the relative penalties of vehicle sizes. If you are in a vehicle when it is reduced to 0 health, you take a certain number of damage, equal to the damage dice listed on the table below.

Vehicle Dodge Penalties  
Small: \-5  
Medium: \-10  
Large: \-15  
Massive: \-20

Vehicle Sizes  
Small: 5x5 feet  
Medium: 10x10 feet  
Large: 15x15 feet  
Massive: 20x20 feet or larger

These sizes are accounting for a grid where each square is 5x5 feet.

Vehicle Destruction Damage  
When a vehicle is destroyed, creatures inside and near the vehicle will take a large amount of damage as the vehicle explodes around them. Each vehicle has a different amount of damage, Dodge DC and radius of explosion. Creatures inside the vehicle take full damage on a failed dodge, and half damage (rounded down) on a success. All creatures in the radius take half damage (rounded down) on a failed dodge and no damage on a success. The different stats for each size are as follows:

**Small:**   
Damage: 5d12  
Dodge DC: 65  
Radius: 5 feet  
**Medium:**   
	Damage: 10d12  
Dodge DC: 75  
Radius: 10 feet  
**Large:**   
Damage: 15d12  
Dodge DC: 85  
Radius: 10 feet  
**Massive:**   
Damage: 20d12  
Dodge DC: 95  
Radius: 15 feet

Vehicle Damage Reduction  
Since metal is more durable than flesh, vehicles will not take as much damage as normal creatures. All non-explosive damage that is not dealt by another vehicle is halved.

Statistics  
**Health:** The amount of damage a vehicle can take before its destruction. A vehicle’s health is divided between the health of its chassis and the health of its component parts. A vehicle’s components are listed in its stat block. By default, all damage sustained by the vehicle is dealt to its chassis, but the attacker may choose to attack a different component of the vehicle, which damages that component as well as the chassis, potentially disabling that part of the vehicle. Vehicle components as well as their disabled effects are listed below.   
**Shields:** The amount of shields a vehicle has. The shields apply to all components of the vehicle and are lost regardless of which component is damaged.  
**Speed:** How fast the vehicle can move in a turn.  
**Terrain:** Where the vehicle operates (e.g., a helicopter’s terrain would be the air).  
**Size:** How large the vehicle is.  
**Seats:** The number of creatures that can fit in a vehicle. It is divided into pilots, gunners, turrets and passengers. Pilots are the number of people operating and driving the vehicle. Gunners are the number of people that can fire their weapon from the vehicle. Turrets are the number of people that can operate the turrets, and passengers are the number of people that ride in the vehicle without doing anything significant.  
**Turret Type:** The type of turret that is on a vehicle.  
**Ram Damage:** The amount of damage done if you ram someone with the vehicle.  
**Ram Dodge:** The Dodge DC for the ram.  
**Weapon Damage:** The amount of damage the vehicle’s weapon does.  
**Weapon Dodge:** The Dodge DC of the vehicle.  
**Weapon Type:** The type of damage the weapon does.  
**Attacks in a Turn:** The number of attacks the vehicle can take in a single Operation.  
**Weapon Range:** The range of the vehicle’s weapon.  
**Special Abilities:** Any abilities the vehicle has that aren’t universal among all vehicles.

Vehicle Components  
When making an attack against different vehicle components, you may add the called shot bonus of the weapon to your attack, however the bonus granted cannot bring the penalty to more than \-0. Additionally, any abilities that allow you to target 2 or more targets, such as *Split* or *Twice the Pride*, can allow you to target multiple components according to how many targets you may attack.   
   
**Axles:** For vehicles that do not rely on flight as their Primary means of locomotion, they are propelled by either treads or tires, which are in turn driven by axles. In this context, the component of Axles refers rather to the tires or treads themselves as opposed to the actual drive shaft(s).   
	*Dodge DC Penalty*: \-10  
	*Disable Effect*: When a vehicle’s axles are disabled the movement of that vehicle is  
	reduced to 0\.  
**Cockpit:** Some vehicles provide extra protection for their pilots in the form of a cockpit. Cockpits are enclosed metal and/or glass structures that surround the pilot, shielding them from harm.   
	*Dodge DC Penalty:* \-10  
	*Disable Effect:* When a vehicle’s cockpit is disabled, the vehicle’s pilot becomes exposed   
	and can be attacked directly with the same \-10 Dodge DC penalty. In addition, once the  
	vehicle's cockpit is disabled, or if it doesn’t have a cockpit, the vehicle can be hijacked.   
**Engine:** A vehicle’s engine is its Primary driving force. An engine is usually contained within the vehicle itself but often parts such as thrusters, exhausts, and other parts are exposed.   
	*Dodge DC Penalty:* \-25  
	*Disable Effect:* When a vehicle’s engine is disabled, roll a d10. On a 1, the vehicle   
	explodes, and is destroyed, triggering the necessary damage roll for vehicle   
	destruction. Otherwise, the vehicle’s speed is halved (rounded down)   
	and its dodge penalty is doubled.  
**Turrets:** In addition to built-in weaponry, some vehicles also possess a turret that can be operated by someone other than the pilot. The most common types are chaingun turrets and plasma cannons, but can include any other type of turret, such as gauss turrets. If a vehicle has multiple turrets, then each turret must be disabled individually.  
*Dodge DC Penalty*: \-5  
*Disable Effect*: When a vehicle’s turret is disabled, the turret can no longer be used to   
make attacks.   
**Wings:** Flying vehicles are kept aloft by their wings. A vehicle with this component may not have wings in the traditional sense, but instead rotors, repulsors, or thrusters that serve a similar function.   
	*Dodge DC Penalty:* \-15  
	*Disable Effect:* When a vehicle’s wings are disabled, its speed is halved (rounded down) 	  
	and its dodge penalty is doubled. In addition, on the start of each of the pilot’s turns, roll   
	a d6. On a 1, if the vehicle has not landed, it crashes to the ground, with both vehicle   
and pilot taking 6 (1d10) of damage for every 10 feet fallen, in a random location determined   
by the GM within the vehicle’s maximum speed. All creatures in the vicinity of the crash  
 (GM’s discretion) are treated as if they had been targeted by the vehicle’s ram attack  
 and must make relevant dodge rolls to avoid the associated damage.   
**Weapons Systems:** Vehicles equipped for war often have built-in weapons and artillery that are operated by the vehicle’s pilot. This could include such weapons as a tank’s cannon or a falcon’s machine guns.   
	*Dodge DC Penalty*: \-20  
	*Disable Effect*: When a vehicle’s weapons systems are disabled, the vehicle’s pilot loses   
the ability to make attacks with the vehicle’s weapons.

Hijacking  
In many situations a player or creature may attempt to hijack a vehicle. Hijacking involves a creature outside of a vehicle attempting to forcefully remove one of the vehicle’s pilots. In order to do this, the creature attempting to hijack the vehicle must be within 5 feet of the vehicle and make an Agility or Handling interaction as a Primary Operation to climb onto the vehicle, followed by a Lifting check, also as a Primary Operation, to pull one pilot out of the vehicle, contested by another Lifting check made by the pilot. If the creature attempting the Hijack succeeds, the Pilot is pulled from the vehicle and falls to the ground to any unoccupied space within 5 feet of the vehicle and is exposed to the Fallen effect. If the creature attempting the hijack fails, they must reroll their Agility interaction to continue to hold on the vehicle or fall to the ground into an unoccupied space within 5 feet of the vehicle and be exposed to the Fallen effect. The DC for the Agility interaction is typically determined by the size of the vehicle (see the table below), modified by an additional \+10 if the vehicle is flying. 

**Small:** DC 90  
**Medium:** DC 75  
**Large:** DC 60  
**Massive:** DC 45

(These values can be altered at the GM’s discretion)

Vehicle Operations  
While driving a vehicle, you cannot make Combat Maneuvers (unless otherwise stated by the vehicle’s Stat Block), but you gain access to a new set of options for your Operation. They are as follows:  
**Entering/Exiting a Vehicle:** Primary Operation and all remaining movement speed with a minimum of 5 feet  
**Using the Vehicle’s Weapons:** Primary Operation  
**Ram:** Secondary Operation (provided that you have moved at least 20 feet towards the target in that turn)  
**Moving the Vehicle:** Tertiary Operation

Ram  
When you successfully hit another vehicle with a Ram attack, your own vehicle takes damage equal to half of the damage dealt (rounded down). 

Combat Maneuvers  
Unless otherwise stated in the vehicle’s stat block, vehicles are not capable of using any combat maneuvers.

Effects Immunity  
Unless otherwise stated, all vehicles are immune to the Blinded, Deafened, Frightened, Grappled, Indomitable, Poisoned, and Unconscious effects.

Stationary  
When a vehicle is not being piloted, it is stationary and suffers a \-25 to all dodges.

*Evasion*: The Seraph can use the Evasion maneuver.

*Armor Plating*: Any time the Wraith is attacked, roll a d6. On a one, the Wraith takes no damage.

### PROMETHEAN VEHICLES

Phaeton  
Health: 400 (Chassis)  
N/A (Axles)  
125 (Cockpit)  
	70 (Engine)  
	N/A (Turrets)  
	100 (Wings)

Turret Type: N/A

Ram Dodge: DC 30  
Weapon Damage: 6d4  
Weapon Dodge: 45  
Weapon Type: Automatic  
Attacks in a Turn: 3  
Weapon Range: 75 feet

**Special Abilities:**  
*Teleportation*: As a Secondary Operation, the Phaeton can teleport to an unoccupied space it can see within 30 feet.   
*Missile Barrage:* The Phaeton is equipped with eight missiles. As a Primary Operation, the pilot may fire up to two of these missiles at a time. Each missile deals 22 (4d10) explosive damage and has a Dodge DC of 35, or Dodge DC 70 if the target is a vehicle, as the missiles home in on the target. Any creatures or vehicles within 5 feet of the target must make a dodge or take half damage (rounded down), taking no damage on a successful dodge.

## GUN ATTACHMENTS

Along the way, your fireteam may find or craft attachments for their weapons or armor that grant them new abilities or make existing ones even better. However, given that the UNSC does not know how Promethean or Covenant weapons function, they can only craft attachments for themselves. Attachments can be found through certain areas on Earth and her colonies, as well as on battlefields and possibly dead bodies. Each weapon can only have one attachment of each Tier at a given time, but can be swapped out at any time using a Primary Operation.

Recommended Ranks For Gun Attachments  
These are the recommended ranks at which Spartans should receive different tiers of gun attachments. These are merely suggested and can be changed as the GM desires.

Tier 1: 1st Lieutenant  
Tier 2: Major  
Tier 3: Colonel Major  
Tier 4: Lieutenant General  
Tier 5: Commander  
Tier 6: Hyper-Lethal Vector

Magnum Pistol  
**Tier I Attachment:**  
*Extended Magazine:* You may reroll 2 Ammo Die per downtime.  
*Improved Storage:* Add \+2 Ammo Dice.  
*Flashlight:* Sheds bright light in a 15 foot cone and can be activated or deactivated as a Tertiary Operation.  
**Tier II Attachment:**  
*Barrel Stabilizer:* Add \+10 feet of range.  
**Tier III Attachment:**  
*Impact Rounds:* Add \+4 (1d6) damage to all damage dealt.  
*Armor Piercing Rounds:* Add \+5 (1d8) to all damage dealt against shields.  
*High Caliber Rounds:* Add \+5 (1d8) to all damage dealt against health.  
**Tier IV Attachment:**  
*Laser Sights:* Increase the Dodge DC by \+10.  
*Customized Holster:* The Magnum Pistol now costs 0 gun slots.  
**Tier V Attachment:**  
*Hair Trigger:* You may make an additional attack with this weapon.  
*Penetrant Rounds:* Cover Negation increases to Average.  
**Tier VI Attachment:**  
*Textured Grip:* You can both switch to the Magnum Pistol and reload it using no Operation, and when being dual wielded, you may make one extra attack with the Magnum Pistol as a second weapon.

Sidekick Pistol  
**Tier I Attachment:**  
*Extended Magazine:* You may reroll 2 Ammo Die per downtime.  
*Improved Storage:* Add \+2 Ammo Die.  
*Flashlight:* Sheds bright light in a 15 foot cone and can be activated or deactivated as a Tertiary Operation.  
**Tier II Attachment:**  
*Barrel Stabilizer:* Add \+10 feet of range.  
**Tier III Attachment:**  
*Impact Rounds:* Add \+6 (1d10) damage to any damage dealt.  
*Armor Piercing Rounds:* Add \+7 (1d12) to any damage dealt against shields.  
*High Caliber Rounds:* Add \+7 (1d12) to any damage dealt against health.  
**Tier IV Attachment:**  
*Laser Sights:* Increase the Dodge DC by \+10.  
*Customized Holster:* The Sidekick Pistol now costs 0 gun slots.  
**Tier V Attachment:**  
*Hair Trigger:* You may make an additional attack with this weapon.  
*Penetrant Rounds:* Cover Negation increases to Weak.  
**Tier VI Attachment:**  
*Textured Grip:* You can both switch to the Sidekick Pistol and reload it using no Operation, and when being dual wielded, you may make one extra attack with the Sidekick Pistol as a second weapon.

SMG (Submachine Gun)  
**Tier I Attachment:**  
*Extended Magazine:* You may reroll 5 Ammo Die per downtime.  
*Improved Storage*: Add \+5 Ammo Die.  
*Flashlight:* Sheds bright light in a 15 foot cone and can be activated or deactivated as a Tertiary Operation.  
**Tier II Attachment:**  
*Barrel Stabilizer:* Add \+10 feet of range.  
**Tier III Attachment:**  
*Impact Rounds:* Add \+1d2 damage to any damage dealt.  
*Armor Piercing Rounds:* Add \+3 (1d4) to any damage dealt against shields.  
*High Caliber Rounds:* Add \+3 (1d4) to any damage dealt against health.  
**Tier IV Attachment:**  
*Laser Sights:* Increase the Dodge DC by \+10.  
*Customized Holster:* The SMG now costs 0 gun slots.  
**Tier V Attachment:**  
*Hair Trigger:* You may make an additional attack with this weapon.  
*Penetrant Rounds:* Cover Negation increases to Weak.  
**Tier VI Attachment:**  
*Textured Grip:* You can both switch to the SMG and reload it using no Operation, and when being dual wielded, you may make one extra attack with the SMG as a second weapon.

Sticky Detonator  
**Tier I Attachment:**  
*Extended Magazine:* You may reroll 1 Ammo Die per downtime.  
*Improved Storage:* Add \+1 Ammo Die.  
*Flashlight:* Sheds bright light in a 15 foot cone and can be activated or deactivated as a Tertiary Operation.  
**Tier II Attachment:**  
*Barrel Stabilizer:* Add \+5 feet of range.  
**Tier III Attachment:**  
*Improved Gunpowder:* Add \+5 radius.  
*Improved Explosives:* Add \+6 (1d10) to all damage.  
*Destructive Detonation:* Add \+11 (2d10) to all damage dealt to vehicles.  
**Tier IV Attachment:**  
*Speedy Reload:* You can reload the Sticky Detonator using no Operation.  
**Tier V Attachment:**  
*Laser Sights:* Increase the Dodge DC by \+10.  
*Shrapnel:* Any creatures within 5 feet of the target take full damage on a failed dodge and half damage (rounded down) on a successful dodge.  
**Tier VI Attachment:**  
*Airborne Charge:* Any creature stuck with the Sticky Detonator must make an additional DC 50 dodge, or take the maximum damage die allowed by a fully charged blast, provided it hasn’t already detonated.

Assault Rifle  
**Tier I Attachment:**  
*Extended Magazine:* You may reroll 4 Ammo Die per downtime.  
*Improved Storage:* Add \+4 Ammo Die.  
*Flashlight:* Sheds bright light in a 15 foot cone and can be activated or deactivated as a Tertiary Operation.  
**Tier II Attachment:**  
*Barrel Stabilizer:* Add \+15 feet of range.  
**Tier III Attachment:**  
*Impact Rounds:* Add \+4 (1d6) damage to any damage dealt.  
*Armor Piercing Rounds:* Add \+5 (1d8) to any damage dealt against shields.  
*High Caliber Rounds:* Add \+5 (1d8) to any damage dealt against health.  
**Tier IV Attachment:**  
*Laser Sights:* Increase the Dodge DC by \+10.  
*Sonic Blast:* Instead of making an attack with this weapon, the assault rifle can be used to produce a sonic shockwave. Any creatures in a 15 foot cone must succeed on the dodge or be exposed to the Deafened effect for 3 turns. This can be done 5 times per downtime.  
**Tier V Attachment:**  
*Hair Trigger:* You may make an additional attack with this weapon.  
*Penetrant Rounds:* Cover Negation increases to Average.  
**Tier VI Attachment:**  
*Scope:* Add \+10 Called Shot Bonus.  
*Grenade Underbarrel:* In exchange for a single attack with this weapon, you can fire a single frag grenade with a 40 foot range. You can store up to 4 grenades at one time and it takes a Secondary Operation to reload each grenade.

Battle Rifle  
**Tier I Attachment:**  
*Extended Magazine:* You may reroll 3 Ammo Die per downtime.  
*Improved Storage:* Add \+3 Ammo Die.  
*Flashlight:* Sheds bright light in a 15 foot cone and can be activated or deactivated as a Tertiary Operation.  
**Tier II Attachment:**  
*Barrel Stabilizer:* Add \+15 feet of range  
**Tier III Attachment:**  
*Impact Rounds:* Add \+5 (1d8) damage to any damage dealt.  
*Armor Piercing Rounds:* Add \+6 (1d10) to any damage dealt against shields.  
*High Caliber Rounds:* Add \+6 (1d10) to any damage dealt against health.  
**Tier IV Attachment:**  
*Laser Sights:* Increase the Dodge DC by \+10.  
*Bayonet:* In exchange for a single attack with this weapon, you can make a melee attack against a creature within 5 feet dealing 18 (4d8) kinetic damage using the same Dodge DC as the weapon.  
**Tier V Attachment:**  
*Hair Trigger:* You may make an additional attack with this weapon.  
*Penetrant Rounds:* Cover Negation increases to Average.  
**Tier VI Attachments:**  
*Compact Stock:* The Battle Rifle is now small size and obtains the dual wielding trait.  
*Bullet Tracker:* If your first shot hits a creature, the Dodge DC increases by 20 for any other attacks made against them during that turn.

Bulldog  
**Tier I Attachment:**  
*Extended Magazine:* You may reroll 2 Ammo Die per downtime.  
*Improved Storage:* Add \+2 Ammo Die.  
*Flashlight:* Sheds bright light in a 15 foot cone and can be activated or deactivated as a Tertiary Operation.  
**Tier II Attachment:**  
*Barrel Stabilizer:* Add \+10 feet of range.  
*Blunted Bullets:* When hit by an attack, targets within 10 feet are pushed back up to 10 feet if they are size medium or smaller, or up to 5 feet if they are size large.  
**Tier III Attachment:**  
*Impact Rounds:* Add \+7 (1d12) damage to any damage dealt.  
*Armor Piercing Roun*ds: Add \+9 (2d8) to any damage dealt against shields.  
*High Caliber Rounds:* Add \+9 (2d8) to any damage dealt against health.  
**Tier IV Attachment:**  
*Laser Sights:* Increase the Dodge DC by \+10.  
*Plasma Shield:* A portable energy shield is encased within the Bulldog with 50 shield health and can be activated and deactivated as a Secondary Operation. When you fail a dodge by 20 or less while the shield is active, the damage is transferred to the shield. While deactivated, the shield regains 10 shield health at the start of each of your turns.  
**Tier V Attachment:**  
*Hair Trigger:* You may make an additional attack with this weapon.  
*Penetrant Rounds:* Cover Negation increases to Average.  
**Tier VI Attachments:**  
*Enlarged Barrel:* The Bulldog adds \+15 to called shots when within 10 feet of the target.  
*Compact Stock:* The Bulldog is now small size and obtains the dual wielding trait.

When you fail a dodge by 20 or less while the shield is active, the damage is transferred to the shield. While deactivated, the shield regains 10 shield health at the start of each of your turns.
