SAW (Squad Automatic Weapon)  
**Tier I Attachment:**  
*Extended Magazine:* You may reroll 2 Ammo Die per downtime.  
*Improved Storage:* Add \+1 Ammo Die.  
*Flashlight:* Sheds bright light in a 15 foot cone and can be activated or deactivated as a Tertiary Operation.  
**Tier II Attachment:**  
*Barrel Stabilizer:* Add \+10 feet of range.  
*Blunted Bullets:* When hit by an attack, targets within 10 feet are pushed back up to 10 feet if they are size medium or smaller, or up to 5 feet if they are size large.  
**Tier III Attachment:**  
*Impact Rounds:* Add \+4 (1d6) damage to any damage dealt.  
*Armor Piercing Rounds:* Add \+5 (1d8) to any damage dealt against shields.  
*High Caliber Rounds:* Add \+5 (1d8) to any damage dealt against health.  
**Tier IV Attachment:**  
*Laser Sights:* Increase the Dodge DC by \+10.  
*Sonic Blast:* Instead of making an attack with this weapon, the assault rifle can be used to produce a sonic shockwave. Any creatures in a 15 foot cone must succeed on the dodge or be exposed to the Deafened effect for 3 turns. This can be done 5 times per downtime.  
**Tier V Attachment:**  
*Hair Trigger:* You may make an additional attack with this weapon.  
*Penetrant Rounds:* Cover Negation increases to Sturdy.  
**Tier VI Attachment:**  
*Overheating Chamber:* After losing an ammo die, the heat generated by the continuous firing is stored in a second chamber, and can be released as a Secondary Operation, emitting fire in a 10 foot line that deal 4 (1d6) Thermal damage for each ammo die lost during that combat encounter, to a maximum of 4d6. The Dodge DC for this attack is equal to the weapon’s Dodge DC. After being used once, the damage resets to 0 and further ammo die must be lost for the attack to be used.   
*Grenade Underbarrel:* In exchange for a single attack with this weapon, you may fire a single frag grenade with a 40 foot range. You can store up to 4 grenades at one time and it takes a Secondary Operation to reload each grenade.

Railgun  
**Tier I Attachment:**  
*Extended Magazine:* You may reroll 1 Ammo Die per downtime.  
*Improved Storage:* Add \+1 Ammo Die.  
*Flashlight:* Sheds bright light in a 15 foot cone and can be activated or deactivated as a Tertiary Operation.  
**Tier II Attachment:**  
*Improved Rifling:* Add \+10 feet of range.  
**Tier III Attachment:**  
*Stunning Blast:* If the target fails the dodge by 50 or more they are exposed to the Stunned effect until the start of their next turn.  
*Deafening Blast:* If the target fails the dodge by 40 or more they are exposed to the Deafened effect until the end of their next turn.   
*Blinding Blast:* If the target fails the dodge by 40 or more they are exposed to the Blinded effect until the end of their next turn.  
*Improved Blast:* Add \+11 (1d20) to all damage dealt.  
**Tier IV Attachment:**  
*Laser Sights:* Increase the Dodge DC by \+10.  
*Homing Chip:* Increase the Dodge DC by \+25 when attacking vehicles.  
**Tier V Attachment:**  
*Wounding Shot:* Any creature who takes 40 or more damage from a single attack is exposed to the Wounded effect for 2 rounds or until they regain any health.  
*Electric Charge:* Any creatures within 5 feet of a creature hit by the Railgun must make a DC 50 dodge or take half of the damage (rounded down).  
*Penetrant Rounds:* Cover Negation increases to Strong.  
**Tier VI Attachment:**  
*Penetrating Shells:* Any creature directly behind another creature hit by the Railgun must make a dodge equal to the Dodge DC of the Railgun \-10 for each creature already hit or take damage equal to the damage dealt by the Railgun \-1 damage die for each creature already hit. The penetration ends when there are no more creatures within range or when potential damage reaches 0\.

Grenade Launcher  
**Tier I Attachment:**  
*Extended Magazine:* You may reroll 1 Ammo Die per downtime.  
*Improved Storage:* Add \+1 Ammo Die.  
*Flashlight:* Sheds bright light in a 15 foot cone and can be activated or deactivated as a Tertiary Operation  
**Tier II Attachment:**  
*Improved Rifling:* Add \+5 feet of range.  
**Tier III Attachment:**  
*Improved Gunpowder:* Add \+5 radius.  
*Improved Explosives:* Add \+7 (1d12) to all damage.  
*Destructive Detonation:* Add \+13 (2d12) to all damage dealt to vehicles.  
**Tier IV Attachment:**  
*Speedy Reload:* You can reload the Grenade Launcher using no Operation.  
*Incendiary Rounds:* Creatures that take damage from a Grenade Launcher’s attack take an additional \+4 (1d6) Thermal Damage.   
**Tier V Attachment:**  
*Laser Sights:* Increase the Dodge DC by \+10.  
*Shrapnel:* Any creatures within 5 feet of the target take full damage on a failed dodge and half damage (rounded down) on a successful dodge.  
**Tier VI Attachment:**  
*Sticky Rounds:* The projectiles of this weapon attach themselves to objects or creatures that they hit, requiring a DC 70 Lifting check to remove if they do not explode outright. If the attack misses the target creature, the projectile becomes attached to an unoccupied space up to 10 feet behind them. If you hit a creature or object with this weapon, you can use Primary Operation to charge it up, doing more damage. For each Operation you charge it up, it will deal an additional \+13 (2d12) explosive damage to a maximum of \+113 (2d12) explosive damage. Once it reaches this point, it explodes immediately. Additionally, you can use a Secondary Operation to detonate it anytime beforehand on your turn.   
Flamethrower  
**Tier I Attachment:**  
*Extended Cartridge:* You may reroll 1 Ammo Die per downtime.  
*Improved Storage:* Add \+1 Ammo Die.  
*Flashlight:* Sheds bright light in a 15 foot cone and can be activated or deactivated as a Tertiary Operation  
**Tier II Attachment:**  
*Improved Ignition:* Add \+5 feet of range.  
**Tier III Attachment:**  
*Improved Flame:* Add \+4 (1d6) to all damage dealt.  
*Blinding Flame:*  If the target fails the dodge by 30 or more they are exposed to the Blinded effect until the end of their next turn.   
*Debilitating Flame:* Any creature that takes maximum damage from the Flamethrower is exposed to the Wounded effect until they regain health in any way.  
**Tier IV Attachment:**  
*Speedy Reload:* You can reload the Flamethrower using no Operation.  
*Empowered Flame:* Increase the Dodge DC by \+10.  
**Tier V Attachment:**  
*Flame Canister:* Cover Negation increases to Weak.   
*Hair Trigger:* You may make an additional attack with this weapon.  
**Tier VI Attachment:**  
*Combustion Chamber:* When making an attack with the Flamethrower, any creature within 5 feet takes an additional \+11 (3d6) Explosive damage on a failed dodge.

Sniper Rifle  
**Tier I Attachment:**  
*Extended Magazine:* You may reroll 1 Ammo Die per downtime.  
*Improved Storage:* Add \+1 Ammo Die.  
*Flashlight:* Sheds bright light in a 15 foot cone and can be activated or deactivated as a Tertiary Operation  
**Tier II Attachment:**  
*Barrel Stabilizer:* Add \+20 feet of range.  
*Adjustable Scope:* You can reliably and accurately see up to 3 miles while looking through your scope.  
**Tier III Attachment:**  
*Impact Rounds:* Add \+6 (1d10) damage to any damage dealt.  
*Armor Piercing Rounds:* Add \+7 (2d6) to any damage dealt against shields.  
*High Caliber Rounds:* Add \+7 (2d6) to any damage dealt against health.  
**Tier IV Attachment:**  
*Laser Sights:* Increase the Dodge DC by \+10.  
*Net Launcher:* As a Primary Operation you can fire a net out of a mounted launcher on your weapon. The target must succeed on a Dodge DC 60 or be exposed to the Incapacitated effect. The net has 20 health and is broken once enough damage is dealt to it. A broken net requires 5 minutes to repair.  
**Tier V Attachment:**  
*Wounding Shot:* Any creature that takes 40 or more damage from a single shot of the Sniper Rifle is exposed to the Wounded effect for 2 rounds or until they regain any health.  
*Penetrant Rounds:* Cover Negation increases to Solid.  
**Tier VI Attachments:**  
*Stabilized Mount:* You may take a Primary Operation to set up your sniper’s mount in a stationary position where you gain the following benefits while set up in this manner:  
	\-Add an extra \+11 (3d6) damage die on a headshot  
	\-Dodge DC increases by 5  
	\-Add \+10 range  
You lose all of these bonuses if you move and take the sniper rifle with you, in which case it requires a Primary Operation to set up again.   
Rocket Launcher  
**Tier I Attachment:**  
*Extra Barrel:* You may reroll 1 Ammo Die per downtime.  
*Improved Storage:* Add \+1 Ammo Die.  
*Flashlight:* Sheds bright light in a 15 foot cone and can be activated or deactivated as a Tertiary Operation

*Speedy Reload:* You can reload the Rocket Launcher using no Operation.  
*Homing Chip:* Add \+25 Dodge DC when attacking vehicles.  
**Tier V Attachment:**  
*Laser Sights:* Increase the Dodge DC by \+10.  
*Shrapnel:* Any creatures within 5 feet of the target take full damage on a failed dodge and half damage (rounded down) on a successful dodge.  
*Blinding Fire:* Any creature who fails the dodge by 35 or more is exposed to the Blinded effect until the end of their next turn.  
*Deafening Wave:* Any creature who fails the dodge by 35 or more is exposed to the Deafened effect until the end of their next turn.  
**Tier VI Attachment:**  
*Wounding Explosives:* Any creature that takes 45 or more damage inside the radius is exposed to the Wounded effect for 2 rounds or until they next regain health.  
*Split Explosives:* Instead of firing normally, you can turn the shell into 3 smaller tracking missiles that are treated as 3 separate attacks, each dealing 2d20 damage with Dodge DC 75\.

Spartan Laser  
**Tier I Attachment:**  
*Extended Energy Capacity:* You may reroll 1 Ammo Die per downtime.  
*Improved Storage:* Add \+1 Ammo Die.  
*Flashlight:* Sheds bright light in a 15 foot cone and can be activated or deactivated as a Tertiary Operation.  
**Tier II Attachment:**  
*Improved Rifling:* Add \+10 feet of range.  
*Crumbling Shot:* Add \+2d20 to all damage dealt to structures.  
**Tier III Attachment:**  
*Stunning Blast:* If the target fails the dodge by 50 or more they are exposed to the Stunned effect until the end of their next turn.  
*Deafening Blast:* If the target fails the dodge by 40 or more they are exposed to the Deafened effect until the end of their next turn.   
*Blinding Blast:* If the target fails the dodge by 40 or more they are exposed to the Blinded effect until the end of their next turn.  
*Improved Blast:* Add \+2d20 to all damage dealt.  
**Tier IV Attachment:**  
*Laser Sights:* Increase the Dodge DC by \+10.  
*Increased Barrel Diameter:* Add \+20 Dodge DC when attacking vehicles.  
*Hull-Piercing Energy:* Add \+4d20 damage to vehicles, but subtract \-2d20 damage from all other damage.  
**Tier V Attachment:**  
*Fast Charge:* Instead of making one attack, you can make two more rapid attacks, each with Dodge DC 50 and dealing 53 (5d20) explosive damage.   
*Shockwave*: The target must make a Dodge DC 65 or be exposed to the Fallen effect. Any creature within 5 feet of the target must make a DC 45 dodge or be exposed to the Fallen effect.   
**Tier VI Attachment:**  
*Penetrating Energy:* Any creature directly behind another creature hit by the Spartan Laser must make a dodge equal to the Dodge DC of the Spartan Laser \-10 for each creature already hit or take damage equal to the damage dealt by the Spartan Laser \-2 damage die for each creature already hit. The penetration ends when there are no more creatures within range or when potential damage reaches 0\.  
*Focusing Lens:* As a Secondary Operation you may adjust a focusing lens in front of the weapon that changes the width of the beam fired. Starting at the weapon’s Dodge DC, for every 5 you increase the Dodge DC you lose \-2d20 damage, and for every 5 you decrease the Dodge DC by you add \+2d20 damag*e*

Hydra Launcher  
**Tier I Attachment:**  
*Extra Barrel:* You may reroll 1 Ammo Die per downtime.  
*Improved Storage:* Add \+1 Ammo Die.  
*Flashlight:* Sheds bright light in a 15 foot cone and can be activated or deactivated as a Tertiary Operation.  
**Tier II Attachment:**  
*Improved Rifling:* Add \+10 feet of range.  
*Crumbling Shot:* Add \+2d20 to all damage dealt to structures.  
**Tier III Attachment:**  
*Impact Explosives:* Add \+6 (1d10) damage to any damage dealt.  
*Armor Piercing Explosives:* Add \+7 (1d12) to any damage dealt against shields.  
*High Caliber Explosives:* Add \+7 (1d12) to any damage dealt against health.  
*Destructive Detonation:* Add \+11 (2d10) to all damage dealt to vehicles.  
**Tier IV Attachment:**  
*Speedy Reload:* You can reload the Hydra Launcher using no Operation.  
*Tracking Homing Chip:* When Homing, add \+25 Dodge DC when attacking vehicles.  
**Tier V Attachment:**  
*Laser Sights:* Add \+10 Dodge DC.  
*Blinding Fire:* Any creature who fails the dodge by 40 or more is exposed to the Blinded effect until the end of their next turn  
*Deafening Wave: A*ny creature who fails the dodge by 40 or more is exposed to the Deafened effect until the end of their next turn.  
*Shrapnel Explosives:* Any creature within 5 feet of the target must make a Dodge DC 40 or take 3d10 kinetic damage.  
**Tier VI Attachment:**  
*Wounding Explosives:* Any creature that takes 45 or more damage in a single attack is exposed to the Wounded effect for two rounds or until they regain any health.  
*Fast Charge:* While homing in on a target, you may spend a Secondary Operation to home in on a second target. 

## TURRET ATTACHMENTS

Turret attachments are more powerful than standard gun attachments. Due to this, there are only three tiers of turret attachments. 

Recommended Ranks For Gun Attachments  
These are the recommended ranks at which Spartans should receive different tiers of gun attachments. These are merely suggested and can be changed as the GM desires.

Tier 1: Major (Equivalent to a tier 2 gun attachment)  
Tier 2: Lieutenant General (Equivalent to a tier 4 gun attachment)  
Tier 3: Hyper-Lethal Vector (Equivalent to a tier 6 gun attachment)

Chaingun Turret  
**Tier I Attachment:**  
*Improved Function:* Add \+2 Ammo Die and \+10 feet of range.  
*Crumbling Barrage:* Deals the normal amount of damage to vehicles.  
*Movement Modification:* Once per turn when the target is hit choose to move them back 10 feet or reduce their movement speed by 10 feet.  
**Tier II Attachment:**  
*Rapid Fire:* You may make an additional attack with this weapon.  
*Impact Rounds:* Add \+1d8 damage to any damage dealt.  
*Laser Sights:* Add \+10 Dodge DC.   
**Tier III Attachment:**  
*Rotating Barrel:* If you spend a Primary Operation you can rev up your barrel. As long as you shoot your chaingun turret on every subsequent turn you deal \+2d8, gain a \+5 to Dodge DC, and gain one additional attack.  
*Flamethrower Underbarrel:* As you fire your weapon, the heat from the barrel is stored in a capsule underneath the chaingun turret. As a Primary Operation you may unleash the stored heat as flame in a 20 foot line. Any creature within that line must make a Dodge DC 60 or take an amount of Thermal Damage equal to the amount rolled on however many ammo dice you have expended, with a maximum of 3d20.

Gauss Turret  
**Tier I Attachment:**  
*Improved Function:* Add \+2 Ammo Die and \+10 feet of range.  
*Crumbling Barrage:* Deals \+3d10 damage to vehicles.  
*Movement Modification:* Once per turn when the target is hit you may choose to push them back up to 10 feet or reduce their movement speed by 10 feet.  
**Tier II Attachment:**  
*Rapid Fire:* You may make an additional attack with this weapon.  
*Impact Rounds:* Add \+1d10 damage to any damage dealt.  
*Laser Sights:* Add \+10 Dodge DC.   
**Tier III Attachment:**  
*Explosive Intent:* Upon killing a target you can choose to force the target to explode. All enemies within 5 feet must succeed a Dodge DC 75, and you and all allies must succeed a Dodge DC 45\. On a failure enemies take 4d10, and on a success they take half. Allies take 2d10 on a failure and no damage on a success.   
*Penetration:* The Gauss Turret now has a Strong cover negation and any creature directly behind your target must also make a dodge equal to the Gauss turret’s Dodge DC \-10 or also take the same amount of damage as the target creature.

Rocket Turret  
**Tier I Attachment:**  
*Improved Function:* Add \+2 Ammo Die and \+10 feet of range.  
*Crumbling Barrage:* Deals \+2d20 damage to structures and vehicles.  
*Movement Modification:* Once per turn when the target is hit choose to move them back 10 feet or reduce their movement speed by 10 feet.  
**Tier II Attachment:**  
*Rapid Fire:* You may make an additional attack with this weapon.  
*Damage Buff:* Add \+ 1d20 damage to any damage dealt.  
*Dodge DC Buff:* Add \+10 Dodge DC.   
**Tier III Attachment:**  
*Splinter Shot:* Increase the Detonation radius of the Rocket Turret to 10 feet.  
*Homing Shots:* You may choose to add \+15 Dodge DC and take a \-1d20 penalty to damage. 

# Allies and Enemies

![][image4]

## ALLY AND ENEMY STATISTICS

In your missions as a fireteam, you will likely encounter many creatures, both hostile and friendly. Some will aid you in battle, but most will stand in the way to your objective. The statistics for these creatures is listed below.

Creature Sizes  
Small: Smaller than 5x5 feet  
Medium: 5x5 feet  
Large: 10x10 feet  
Massive: 15x15 feet or larger

These sizes are accounting for a grid where each square is 5x5 feet.

Statistics Guide  
Creature’s Name (Classification)

| Core | Offensive | Support |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| **Race:** The creature’s race. **Classification:** The creature’s classification or rank within their race. **Health:** The amount of health a creature has. **Shields:** The amount of shields a creature has. **Dodge Bonus:** The creature’s dodge bonus. **Size:** The creature’s size **Speed:** The creature’s speed. This will also designate whether or not the creature can fly. | **Melee Dodge DC:** The creature’s Dodge DC of their melee attack **Melee Damage:** The damage of the creature’s melee attack on a hit **Grenades:** The number and type of grenades the creature has. **Available Weaponry:** The weapons that the creature has access to. It is recommended that each creature only has 2 or 3 weapons equipped at a time, regardless of how many may be available to them.  | **Superiorities (+?):** The creature’s interaction Superiorities and Superiority bonus. **Expertises (+?):** The creature’s interaction Expertises and Expertise bonus. **Weapon Superiorities:** The creature’s Weapon Superiorities. **Weapon Expertises:** The Creature’s Weapon Expertises. **Effect Immunities:** The Effects that the creature is immune to. |
| **Innate Skills** | **Passive Skills** | **Operational Skills** |
| Innate Skills are abilities tied to the creature’s race or classification. | Passive Skills are non-Innate abilities that do not require the use of any Operations. | Operational skills are non-Innate abilities that require the use of Operations |

Combat Maneuvers  
Unless otherwise stated in the creature’s stat block, creatures are not capable of using any combat maneuvers.

Weapon Superiority and Expertise  
Many creatures have superiority or expertise in certain weapons and will thus be significantly more efficient with them. The bonuses they get are dependent on the size of the weapon and are as follows:

**Weapon Superiority**  
Small/Medium: \+1 damage die, \+5 Dodge DC  
Large/Massive: \+2 damage die, \+10 Dodge DC

**Weapon Expertise**  
Small/Medium: \+3 damage die, \+10 Dodge DC  
Large/Massive: \+4 damage die, \+20 Dodge DC

Drone (Minor)

Huragok

| **Innate Skills** | **Passive Skills** | **Operational Skills** |
| N/A | **Overshield:** All allies have their maximum shield capacity double while within 50 feet of the Huragok, or if they do not have shields, they instead receive maximum shields equal to their base maximum health while in range. These additional shields are removed when the Huragok dies. **Suicide:** If the Huragok falls below 20 health but is not killed, on its next turn it will use all of its movement towards the nearest target and explode, whether or not it reaches the target. If the target is within 5 feet, it must make a Dodge DC 70 or take 28 (5d10) Explosive damage, or half as much on a success (rounded down). Any other creatures within 5 feet of the Huragok must also make a Dodge DC 70\. On a failure, they take half damage (rounded down), taking no damage on a success. | **Disable:** As a Primary Operation, the Huragok can temporarily render 1 electronic device or weapon that it can touch unusable for up to a 1 hour. **Protector:** The Huragok can end 1 effect that isn’t the Wounded effect on an ally it can touch as a Secondary Operation. |

| **Unique Weapon:** The Hunter uses the Assault Cannon attached to its arm to make all weapon attacks. **Deployed in Pairs:** They are never alone, as they are always deployed in sets of two. **Rage:** When one Hunter is killed and its partner is still alive, the remaining Hunter gains the following enhancements; Receives \+100 health. Dodge bonus increases to \+5. Movement speed increases by \+10 feet. Whenever the Hunter makes an attack with its Assault Cannon, it can make a melee attack as a Secondary Operation. | ***Shielded:*** The Hunter has a \+20 to all dodges from attackers that it can see. If the attack would otherwise hit, it hits the shield. The shield has 500 health. **Armored:** All damage dealt to the Hunter is halved unless the hunter fails the dodge by 40 or more, is dealt explosive damage or is exposed to the Surprised Effect. | N/A |

Assault Cannon (Hunter Weapon)  
Damage: 8d20  
Dodge: DC 50  
Size: Massive  
Type: Explosive, Plasma  
Maximum Ammo Storage: N/A  
Shots per Magazine: N/A  
Attacks: 1  
Dual-Wield: No  
Precision Weapon: No  
Range: 50 feet

**Special Abilities:**  
*Detonation:* The target creature must make a dodge or take full damage, taking half damage (rounded down) on a success. Any creature within 5 feet of the detonation must make a dodge or take half damage (rounded down), taking no damage on a success.

Add \+10 Dodge DC for any attacks made with the vehicle's weapons. The DC for Agility checks related to hijacking increases by 30\. The vehicle’s health increases by an amount determined by the vehicle’s size: Small Vehicles: \+40 health. Medium Vehicles: \+80 health. Large Vehicles: \+120 health. Massive Vehicles: \+160 health. | **Brutal Resilience:** Once, as a Primary, Secondary, and Tertiary Operation, the Brute (Shipmaster) can regain 33 (6d10) health. **Resist:** As a reactionary Operation, after being hit by an attack the Brute (Shipmaster) can roll 1d12 and subtract the result from the damage taken. |

Brute (Army Commander)

| Core | Offensive | Support |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| **Race:** Jiralhanae (Brute) **Classification:** Army Commander **Health:** 160 **Shields:** 80 **Dodge Bonus:** \+10 **Size:** Medium **Speed:** 30 feet | **Melee Dodge DC:** 75 **Melee Damage:** 41 (9d8) Kinetic **Grenades:** 4 (Incendiary) **Available Weaponry:** Skewer, Brute shot, Ravager, Spiker | **Superiorities (+25):** Firepower, Detection, History, Charisma **Expertises (+50):** Fortitude, Lifting, Tactics **Weapon Superiorities:** Spiker, Brute Shot, Ravager **Weapon Expertises:** Skewer **Effect Immunities:** Frightened |
| **Innate Skills** | **Passive Skills** | **Operational Skills** |
| **Charge:** As a Secondary and Tertiary Operations the Brute (Army Commander) can move half of their movement speed (rounded down) and gain an additional \+15 Dodge bonus against Chance Attacks. **Grab:** If the Brute (Army Commander) hits a melee attack, they may immediately take the Grapple combat maneuver, expending only a Secondary and Tertiary Operation. ***Frenzy:*** When the Brute (Army Commander) reaches 40 health or lower, they take only half damage (rounded down) from Kinetic, Hardlight, and Plasma damage, and their melee damage increases by \+9 (2d8) damage die. | **Alpha:** Whenever the Brute (Army Commander) hits an attack they choose 1 ally and that ally deals \+1 additional damage die on their next attack. **Vicious:** If the Brute (Army Commander) deals more than 60 damage in a turn to a single target, that creature is exposed to the Wounded effect until they regain health in any way or complete a downtime. **Menacing:** Enemy creatures within 20 feet of the Brute (Army Commander) must make a DC 55 Fortitude interaction or be exposed to the Frightened effect. Each creature affected by this can remake the Fortitude interaction roll at the end of each turn. A creature that succeeds its interaction roll becomes immune to this effect for 24 hours.  **Unwavering Presence:** Any allies that can see the Brute (Army Commander) are immune to the Frightened effect.  | **Brutal Resilience:** Once, as a Primary, Secondary, and Tertiary Operation, the Brute (Army Commander) can regain 33 (6d10) health. **Resist:** As a reactionary Operation, after being hit by an attack the Brute (Army Commander) can roll 1d12 and subtract the result from the damage taken. **Callout:** Once per round, as a Secondary Operation, the Brute (Army Commander) may choose 1 ally that it can see within 60 feet. The next time that ally makes an attack, they may roll 11 (2d10) and increase the Dodge DC of their attack by the amount rolled on the die.  *Resist:* As a reactionary Operation, after being hit by an attack the Brute (Army Commander) can roll 7 (1d12) and subtract the result from the damage taken. |

Brute (Chieftain)

| Core | Offensive | Support |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| **Race:** Jiralhanae (Brute) **Classification:** Chieftain **Health:** 200 **Shields:** 100 **Dodge Bonus:** \+10 **Size:** Medium **Speed:** 30 feet | **Melee Dodge DC:** 80 **Melee Damage:** 45 (10d8) Kinetic **Grenades:** 4 (Incendiary) **Available Weaponry:** Fuel Rod Cannon, Gravity Hammer, Skewer, Brute Shot, Spiker | **Superiorities (+30):** Detection, History, Charisma **Expertises (+60):** Fortitude, Lifting, Tactics, Firepower **Weapon Superiorities:** Skewer, Brute Shot, Spiker **Weapon Expertises:** Fuel Rod Cannon, Gravity Hammer **Effect Immunities:** Frightened |
| **Innate Skills** | **Passive Skills** | **Operational Skills** |
| **Charge:** As a Secondary and Tertiary Operations the Brute (Chieftain) can move half of their movement speed (rounded down) and gain an additional \+15 Dodge bonus against Chance Attacks. **Grab:** If the Brute (Chieftain) hits a melee attack, they may immediately take the Grapple combat maneuver, expending only a Secondary and Tertiary Operation. ***Frenzy:*** When the Brute (Chieftain) reaches 70 health or lower, they take only half damage (rounded down) from Kinetic, Hardlight, and Plasma damage, and their melee damage increases by \+14 (3d8) damage die. | **Alpha:** Whenever the Brute (Chieftain) hits an attack they choose 1 ally and that ally deals \+1 additional damage die on their next attack. **Vicious:** If the Brute (Chieftain) deals more than 60 damage in a turn to a single target, that creature is exposed to the Wounded effect until they regain health in any way or complete a downtime. **Menacing:** Enemy creatures within 20 feet of the Brute (Chieftain) must make a DC 55 Fortitude interaction or be exposed to the Frightened effect. Each creature affected by this can remake the Fortitude interaction roll at the end of each turn. A creature that succeeds its interaction roll becomes immune to this effect for 24 hours.  **Unwavering Presence:** Any allies that can see the Brute (Chieftain) are immune to the Frightened effect.  **Deadly Attacks:** When their attack hits, the Brute (Chieftain) may roll for damage twice and take the higher result.  **No Weaklings on my Watch:** If an allied Brute within 20 feet of the Brute (Chieftain) is reduced to 0 health, the Brute (Chieftain) may choose to restore them to 1 health. An ally may not benefit from this ability more than once.   | **Brutal Resilience:** Once, as a Primary, Secondary, and Tertiary Operation, the Brute (Chieftain) can regain 46 (8d10) health. **Resist:** As a reactionary Operation, after being hit by an attack the Brute (Chieftain) can roll 1d12 and subtract the result from the damage taken. **Callout:** Once per round, as a Secondary Operation, the Brute (Chieftain) may choose 1 ally that it can see within 60 feet. The next time that ally makes an attack, they may roll 11 (2d10) and increase the Dodge DC of their attack by the amount rolled on the die.   |

Brute (War Chieftain)

| Core | Offensive | Support |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| **Race:** Jiralhanae (Brute) **Classification:** Chieftain **Health:** 250 **Shields:** 150 **Dodge Bonus:** \+10 **Size:** Medium **Speed:** 30 feet | **Melee Dodge DC:** 85 **Melee Damage:** 45 (10d8) Kinetic **Grenades:** 4 (Incendiary) **Available Weaponry:** Fuel Rod Cannon, Gravity Hammer, Skewer, Brute Shot, Spiker | **Superiorities (+30):** Detection, History, Charisma **Expertises (+60):** Fortitude, Lifting, Tactics, Firepower **Weapon Superiorities:** Brute Shot, Spiker **Weapon Expertises:** Fuel Rod Cannon, Gravity Hammer, Skewer **Effect Immunities:** Frightened |
| **Innate Skills** | **Passive Skills** | **Operational Skills** |
| **Charge:** As a Secondary and Tertiary Operations the Brute (War Chieftain) can move half of their movement speed (rounded down) and gain an additional \+15 Dodge bonus against Chance Attacks. **Grab:** If the Brute (War Chieftain) hits a melee attack, they may immediately take the Grapple combat maneuver, expending only a Secondary and Tertiary Operation. ***Frenzy:*** When the Brute (War Chieftain) reaches 85 health or lower, they take only half damage (rounded down) from Kinetic, Hardlight, and Plasma damage, and their melee damage increases by \+14 (3d8) damage die. | **Alpha:** Whenever the Brute (War Chieftain) hits an attack they choose 1 ally and that ally deals \+1 additional damage die on their next attack. **Vicious:** If the Brute (War Chieftain) deals more than 60 damage in a turn to a single target, that creature is exposed to the Wounded effect until they regain health in any way or complete a downtime. **Menacing:** Enemy creatures within 20 feet of the Brute (War Chieftain) must make a DC 65 Fortitude interaction or be exposed to the Frightened effect. Each creature affected by this can remake the Fortitude interaction roll at the end of each turn. A creature that succeeds its interaction roll becomes immune to this effect for 24 hours.  **Unwavering Presence:** Any allies that can see the Brute (War Chieftain) are immune to the Frightened effect.  **Deadly Attacks:** When their attack hits, the Brute (War Chieftain) may roll for damage twice and take the higher result.  **No Weaklings on my Watch:** If an allied Brute within 20 feet of the Brute (War Chieftain) is reduced to 0 health, the Brute (War Chieftain) may choose to restore them to 1 health. An ally may not benefit from this ability more than once.  **Challenge:** When in combat with a creature where there are no other creatures within 5 feet of either the Brute (War Chieftain) and their target, The War Chieftain gains an additional Primary Operation.  | **Brutal Resilience:** Once, as a Primary, Secondary, and Tertiary Operation, the Brute (War Chieftain) can regain 50 (9d10) health. **Resist:** As a reactionary Operation, after being hit by an attack the Brute (War Chieftain) can roll 1d20 and subtract the result from the damage taken. **Callout:** Once per round, as a Secondary Operation, the Brute (War Chieftain) may choose 1 ally that it can see within 60 feet. The next time that ally makes an attack, they may roll 11 (2d10) and increase the Dodge DC of their attack by the amount rolled on the die.  **Rend:** As a Primary Operation, a Brute (War Chieftain) can choose to force a creature grappled by it to make a DC 70 Fortitude interaction, taking 22 (4d10) Kinetic damage and being exposed to the Wounded effect on a failure, or taking 11 (2d10) Kinetic damage and not being exposed to the Wounded effect on a successful interaction. If the creature is already exposed to the Wounded effect, they take 55 (10d10) Kinetic damage on a failure, or 28 (5d10) on a success.   |

|  **Race:** Sangheili (Elite) **Classification:** Zealot **Health:** 50 **Shields:** 150 **Dodge Bonus:** \+10 **Size:** Medium **Speed:** 40 feet | **Melee Dodge DC:** 60 **Melee Damage:** 36 (8d8) Kinetic **Grenades:** 4 (Plasma) **Available Weaponry:** Fuel Rod Cannon, Beam Rifle, Concussion Rifle, Energy Sword, Plasma Rifle, Storm Rifle, Carbine Rifle  | **Superiorities (+20):** Agility, Tracking, Stealth, History **Expertises (+40):** Detection, Tactics, Firepower **Weapon Superiorities:** Beam Rifle, Fuel Rod Cannon, Plasma Rifle, Storm Rifle, Energy Sword **Weapon Expertises:** Concussion Rifle, Carbine Rifle **Effect Immunities:** N/A |
| **Innate Skills** | **Passive Skills** | **Operational Skills** |
| **Nightvision:** The Elite (Zealot) ignores penalties resulting from Darkness. **Honor In Death:** When the Elite (Zealot) is reduced to 0 health, it may roll a d100. If the result of this roll is above 50, the Elite (Zealot) is not killed and drops to 1 health. Each time it uses this ability the DC increases by 20\. **Brotherhood of Warriors:** If an Elite is killed within sight of an Elite (Zealot), the Elite (Zealot) may immediately make a single attack targeted on the creature that killed the Elite, provided they are within range and within line of sight.  | **Zealous Devotion:** Once per turn, when making an attack, the Elite (Zealot) can sacrifice their \+10 Dodge Bonus to impose a \-10 Dodge Penalty on their target, but lose their Dodge Bonus until the start of their next turn.  **Menacing:** Enemy creatures within 20 feet of the Elite (Zealot) must make a DC 45 Fortitude interaction or be exposed to the Frightened effect. Each creature affected by this can remake the Fortitude interaction roll at the end of each turn. A creature that succeeds its interaction roll becomes immune to this effect for 24 hours.  | **Armor Lock:** Once per downtime, as a Primary Operation, the Elite (Zealot) may enter into an armor lock where they stay for up to 2 turns or until the Elite (Zealot) ends it as a Secondary Operation. During this time it suffers a \-50 to all dodges and the Elite (Zealot)’s speed is reduced to 0 feet, but is immune to all damage and negative effects except that which the GM considers unreasonable (such as a nuclear explosion). When the Elite (Field Marshal) exits armor lock any hostile creature within 5 feet of it must succeed on a Dodge DC 80 or take however much damage the Elite (Zealot) took while armor locked as shock damage (Fortitude DC 60), taking half damage (rounded down) on a successful dodge. **Sacrifice:** If an ally within 10 feet of the Elite (Zealot) is hit by an attack, the Elite (Zealot) can choose to make themselves the target of the attack instead as a Reactive Operation, suffering full damage and effects.  |

During this time it suffers a \-50 to all dodges and the Elite (Field Marshal)’s speed is reduced to 0 feet, but is immune to all damage and negative effects except that which the GM considers unreasonable (such as a nuclear explosion). Medium Vehicles: \+80 health. Large Vehicles: \+120 health. Massive Vehicles: \+160 health. **Flagship:** Whenever the Elite (Shipmaster) is onboard a ship under their command they gain the following benefits: They are immune to the Surprised and Frightened effects Creatures within sight of the Elite (Shipmaster) are immune to the Frightened effect | N/A |

Each creature affected by this can remake the Fortitude interaction roll at the end of each turn. | **Promethean Vision:** The Crawler (Alpha) ignores penalties resulting from Darkness, and can see any creature within 60 feet that is not obscured by cover. **Headshot Susceptibility:** Any headshot scored against the Crawler (Alpha) deals \+1 additional damage die. **Bite:** As a Primary Operation, the Crawler (Alpha) can make a bite attack against 1 creature within 5 feet with Dodge DC 40, dealing 20 (3d12) kinetic damage on a hit. **Nimble:** The Crawler (Alpha) can take the Dash maneuver using no Operations. | **Leader of the Pack:** Any Crawler that is aware of the Crawler (Alpha)’s presence within 40 feet is immune to the Frightened effect and gains an additional Secondary and Tertiary Operation.  | N/A  |

## FLOOD ENEMIES

Infection Form

| Core | Offensive | Support |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| **Race:** Flood **Classification:** Infection Form **Health:** 5 **Shields:** N/A **Dodge Bonus:** \+10 **Size:** Tiny **Speed:** 30 feet | **Melee Dodge DC:** 50 **Melee Damage:** 3 (1d4) Acid **Grenades:** N/A **Available Weaponry:** N/A | **Superiorities (+5):**  N/A **Expertises (+10):** N/A **Weapon Superiorities:** N/A **Weapon Expertises:** N/A **Effect Immunities:** Poisoned, Frightened |
| **Innate Skills** | **Passive Skills** | **Operational Skills** |
| **Hive Mind**: The Dodge DC of the Infection Form’s attacks increase by \+5 for each Flood creature within 10 feet of it. **Virus:** When a target is hit by a melee attack from the Infection Form, they must make a DC 50 Fortitude interaction or be exposed to the Poisoned effect. **Flammable:** Infection Forms take double damage from Thermal damage. | **Skitter:** The Infection Form can move freely on walls and ceilings without penalty. **Infection:** When a creature that is exposed to the Poisoned effect is hit by a melee attack from the Infection Form, the target must succeed on a DC 10 Fortitude interaction. Each time the target is hit by an Infection Form’s melee attack, the DC of the Fortitude interaction increases by \+5. On a failure, the target dies and transforms into the Flood form of their race in 3 (1d4) turns. The Infection Form dies if it lands a melee attack. **Spring:** Instead of moving normally, the Infection Form can jump up to 30 feet in any direction from a standing position. | N/A |

If the result of this roll is above 50, the Sangheili Form is not killed and drops to 1 health. Each time it uses this ability the DC increases by 20\. | **Clobber:** The Sangheili Form may spend a Secondary Operation to make a melee attack.   |

On a hit, the target creature is engulfed into the innards of the Juggernaut form, taking 55 (10d10) Acid damage at the start of their turn. Additionally, the creature is exposed to the Blinded and Incapacitated effects as well as having their speed reduced to 0\. Only one creature at a time can be engulfed in this way. If the Juggernaut Form takes 50 or more damage from a single attack, they must make a DC 90 Fortitude interaction or spit out the engulfed creature anywhere within 10 feet, exposing it to the Fallen effect. |

A creature that succeeds its interaction roll becomes immune to this effect for 24 hours.  **Miasma:** Non-Flood Creatures race who start their turn within 10 feet of the Proto-Gravemind are exposed to the Blinded effect for as long as they are within 10 feet of the Proto-Gravemind.  **Blindsight:** The Proto-Gravemind can detect any creature within 60 feet of it without any interaction roll, regardless of an invisibility or any form of obscurity. | **Biomass:** As a Secondary Operation, the Proto-Gravemind can create 6 (1d10) Infection Forms or 3 (1d4) Stalker Forms in an unoccupied space within 10 feet. Any creatures created in this way die when the Proto-Gravemind that created them dies. **Poison:** As a Primary Operation, the Proto-Gravemind can pick a point within 30 feet, forcing all creatures within 5 feet to make a DC 80 Fortitude interaction or be exposed to the Poisoned effect. Any creatures already exposed to the Poisoned effect take an additional 28 (6d10) Acid damage.  **Empower:** As a Primary Operation, the Proto-Gravemind can select 1 Flood creature it can see within 30 feet and expose them to the Indomitable effect until the end of their next turn.   |

Gravemind

| Core | Offensive | Support |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| **Race:** Flood **Classification:** Gravemind Form **Health:** 5000 **Shields:** N/A **Dodge Bonus:** \-20 **Size:** Massive **Speed:** 0 feet | **Melee Dodge DC:** 90 **Melee Damage:** 98 (15d12) Kinetic **Grenades:** N/A **Available Weaponry:** N/A | **Superiorities (+30):** Tech, Firepower, Charisma, Detection, History **Expertises (+60):** Fortitude, Lifting, Tactics **Weapon Superiorities:** N/A **Weapon Expertises:** N/A **Effect Immunities:** Poisoned, Frightened |

| **Enhanced Hive Mind:** The Dodge DC of the Gravemind’s attacks increase by \+10 for each Flood creature within 15 feet of it, along with its Dodge Bonus and interactions that it has Superiority or Expertise in.  **Virus:** When a target is hit by a melee attack from the Gravemind, they must make a DC 80 Fortitude interaction or be exposed to the Poisoned effect. **Flammable:** The Gravemind takes double damage from Thermal damage. | **Hive Mind Nexus**: Any Flood creatures within 60 feet of the Gravemind gain an additional \+30 bonus to their Dodge DCs, dodge Bonus, and movement speed, as well as regaining 3d10 health at the start of each of their turns. **Menacing:** Enemy creatures within 90 feet of the Gravemind must make a DC 100 Fortitude interaction or be exposed to the Frightened effect. Each creature affected by this can remake the Fortitude interaction roll at the end of each turn. A creature that succeeds its interaction roll becomes immune to this effect for 24 hours.  **Miasma:** Non-Flood Creatures race who start their turn within 20 feet of the Gravemind are exposed to the Blinded effect for as long as they are within 20 feet of the Gravemind.  **Blindsight:** The Gravemind can detect any creature within 90 feet of it without any interaction roll, regardless of an invisibility or any form of obscurity. **Grasping Tendrils:** When the Gravemind hits a melee attack against a creature, that creature must make a DC 90 Lifting interaction or be exposed to the Grappled effect. Creatures Grappled by the Gravemind have their speed reduced to 0 and are pulled up to 30 feet in the air where they remain until the Gravemind releases them, until the creature succeeds in a Lifting contest against the Gravemind as a Primary Operation(in which case they fall and are exposed to the Fallen effect), or until a called shot targeting the Gravemind’s tendril (treated as a called shot to an Arm) deals at least 60 damage of any type. The Gravemind may attempt to grapple vehicles as well as creatures in this way. | **Biomass:** As a Secondary Operation, the Gravemind can create 11 (1d20) Infection Forms or 5 (1d8) Stalker Forms in an unoccupied space within 10 feet. Any creatures created in this way die when the Gravemind that created them dies. **Engulf:** As a Primary Operation, the Gravemind may make a melee attack against a creature exposed to the Grappled effect. On a hit, the target creature is engulfed into the innards of the Gravemind, taking 83 (15d10) Acid damage at the start of their turn. Additionally, the creature is exposed to the Blinded and Incapacitated effects as well as having their speed reduced to 0\. Only one creature at a time can be engulfed in this way. If the Gravemind takes 75 or more damage from a single attack, they must make a DC 90 Fortitude interaction or spit out the engulfed creature anywhere within 10 feet, exposing it to the Fallen effect. **Poison:** As a Primary Operation, the Gravemind can pick a point within 50 feet, forcing all creatures within 10 feet to make a DC 80 Fortitude interaction or be exposed to the Poisoned effect. Any creatures already exposed to the Poisoned effect take an additional 44 (8d10) Acid damage.  **Empower:** As a Primary Operation, the Gravemind can select 4 (1d6) Flood creatures it can see within 50 feet and expose them to the Indomitable effect until the end of their next turn. **Disrupt:** As a Primary Operation, the Gravemind can force all creatures within melee range to make a DC 80 Agility interaction or be exposed to the Fallen effect and take 22 (4d10) Kinetic damage  |

## 

## UNSC ALLIES

Ally Combat  
At the GM’s discretion, at least three allies within 30 feet of each other can be organized into squads, meaning that so long as they are within 30 feet of one other ally that is part of that squad, they are counted as a single creature for purposes of initiative, movement, and combat. Before initiative is rolled, the GM may designate a group of allies within this distance to be considered a squad and will roll initiative as if they were a single creature, with no bonuses. When this group is formed, their health is calculated as a unit and is equal to the sum of the health of each of the collective members. Whenever the squad loses an amount of health equal to the squad’s maximum health divided by the number of members, a single ally is removed from the squad. If a squad is reduced to two or fewer members it ceases to be counted as a squad and is counted as individual creatures operating on the same initiative count. On its turn, the squad does not take Operations as normal but instead, deals an amount of damage to any creature of its choice within 50 feet equal to the current health of the squad divided by 4\. The squad has no bonuses to dodges, attacks, or any dice rolls made as a squad.

| **Innate Skills** | **Passive Skills** | **Operational Skills** |
| **Platoon:** If at least 3 other UNSC allies are within 40 feet of the UNSC (ODST Sergeant), they can make 1 additional attack with a weapon of medium size or smaller | **Efficient:** Add \+3 to all attacks made with the Battle Rifle. | **Rally:** As a Primary Operation the UNSC (ODST Sergeant) can roll a d20. All allies within 25 feet regain an amount of health equal to that roll. **Inspire:** As a Secondary and Tertiary Operation, the ODST sergeant can select 1 ally within 30 feet and roll 1d6. The damage of all attacks made by that ally is increased by the amount rolled until the end of that ally’s next turn.  |
